1935.01.17

Main Items in Today's Newspaper

Domestic: Yutian Corps Commander Wang Bingxiao's troops and Security Commander Feng Shoupeng's troops in fierce battle. He Yingqin departs from Taiyuan to return to Peiping.

International: League of Nations Administrative Yuan meeting postponed. The Saar issue creates waves. Soviet Russia holds the Sixteenth National Congress.

Shanghai: Chairman Chiang visits Duan Qirui yesterday morning. The city experiences initial ice formation.

Yutian Troops Clash Violently

Lin Nancang Town Briefly Site of Street Fighting

The Essence of the Entire Town Destroyed by Artillery Fire

Wang Bingxiao's Troops Retreat to Yanshan Pass

Feng Shoupeng's Troops in Active Pursuit

(Peiping) After the rebellion of Wang Bingxiao's Yutian Republic troops, the Security Corps under Feng Shoupeng quelled the situation. They have now retreated to Yanshan Pass and other areas on the border of Ji County and Yutian County. The Security Corps is continuing its pursuit and suppression. In order to resolve this issue, Yin Rugeng went to Tianjin this morning to meet with Yu Xuezhong to request instructions on everything. After reaching a result through consultation, he will return to Peiping within days. (16th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) After the looting of Lin Nancang Town, there was no one at the market on the 14th. The great fire was only extinguished in the afternoon of the 14th. Due to the lack of rescue, the essence of the entire town was burned. The corpses of town police and civilians were scattered throughout the town, with no one to collect them. The scene was extremely tragic. (16th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) A portion of the Yuhong Bridge militia retreated towards the border of Ji County. On the 15th, they arrived at Xin'an Town. Due to obstruction by the Ji County Security Tunnels, they retreated towards Yanshan Pass to regroup. (16th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) This afternoon, Yin Rugeng came to Tianjin from Peiping regarding the clash between Wang Bingxiao's Yutian troop militia and the Security Corps under Feng Shoupeng. He immediately met with Chairman Yu to present a request for a decision on how to handle the situation. He returned to Peiping at 4:00 PM that day and will go to Tongzhou to mediate nearby. (16th Dispatch) (Tianjin) The Yutian troop conflict occurred while Zhu Shiqin was bedridden in Peiping and unable to go and mediate. The provincial government notified Yin Rugeng, who was in Peiping, by telephone to quickly handle the situation, temporarily halt the conflict, and then think of ways for the aftermath. The underlying cause of the Yutian militia and Security Corps conflict is that the troops had deep-seated resentment. The recent cause was that Feng Shoupeng, the special team leader of the Security Corps, fabricated accusations that the militia commander Wang Bingxiao cruelly killed Japanese people and was arrested by the Tangshan military. Wang held great resentment and thought of revenge day and night. (16th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the 15th, Yutian Yahong Bridge Town was surrounded by Sun Yucheng, commander of the Security Supplementary Team. Most of the militia stationed in the town had already retreated with Wang Bingxiao to Yanshan Pass on the border of Ji and Yutian counties. The Security Corps under Feng Shoupeng continued to pursue relentlessly. Fierce fighting had already broken out on the border of Ji and Yutian counties on the evening of the 15th. The Ji Province government has now received a report and has telegraphed Fan Jingyang's First Regiment of the Ji County Security Corps to rush to the border to block the escape of the troops. (16th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) According to information from Yutian, the truth of the troop conflict is that during the morning market in Lin Nancang Town on the 13th, about 350 militiamen from Wang Bingxiao's unit, led by Section Chief Li Weizhou, suddenly infiltrated the town, wearing red ribbons on their lapels and concealing guns. They first surrounded the Chamber of Commerce defense post and disarmed them, then went to the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau and disarmed the police. The head of the branch, Jia Shaoqing, escaped through the back door. The 70-plus members of the Special Forces stationed in the town, under Feng Shoupeng, engaged in street fighting with the militia. After three hours, they were outnumbered, with four killed and the rest disarmed. Upon receiving the report, Feng Shoupeng led his troops to assist Sun Yucheng, the commander of the First Battalion, to rescue, trapping the militia in the town. Using mortars and machine guns, they launched a fierce attack on the town, causing more than a hundred houses in the town to be destroyed by fire. Men and women cried out in shock. The standoff lasted until 8 p.m., when the troops were overwhelmed and suffered heavy casualties. Li Weizhou led a breakout and retreated to Linxi Village west of the town. Feng then led his troops in pursuit, and they retreated to Yanshan Pass. Wang Bingxiao himself is said to be still holed up in Yahong Bridge. (16th Dispatch)

Liu Zuo Zhou Denies

Discord Among Changli and Luan County Troops

(Tianjin) Japanese sources claim that cracks have appeared between the Changli and Luan County militias and the First Regiment of the War Zone Security Corps, creating instability. Today, the Ji Province government received a telegram from Liu Zuozhou, the commander of the Security Corps, reporting that there was no such thing. The militia and security team are very harmonious and have made tight arrangements for winter defense, assisting each other in case of incidents. The Japanese propaganda may have a purpose and should not be believed. Japanese and Korean residents in Changli and Luan County organized volunteer corps. On the 15th, each held an establishment ceremony. Ochiai and Kawai, the captains of the Japanese troops in Shanhaiguan, sent personnel to attend the ceremony. The Changli volunteer

corps consists of thirty members, and Luan County consists of forty, each with retired soldiers as training officers. (16th Dispatch)

(Peiping) According to transportation circles, more than 150 Japanese guards stationed in Yuguan, using the excuse of the Changli security team rioting, traveled from Yu to Changli. However, the Changli security team sent letters to all parties denying any rioting. (16th Dispatch)

Guerrillas Destroyed Labin Road

A Foreign Military Train Overturned and Attacked

(Tianjin) According to news from outside the pass, the railroad tracks between Wuchang and Lalin on the Labin Road were destroyed by guerrillas on the 2nd of this month. A foreign military train traveling in the area was overturned. The guerrillas then launched a surprise attack, raining down bullets. The enemy suffered heavy casualties. The siege was lifted only after reinforcements arrived. (16th, China Press Dispatch)

Luan Dong Mining Area

Five Traitors Captured

(Tianjin) Zhang Xizhe, son of Zhang Haipeng, the puppet Rehe garrison commander, sent his henchmen Biao Rui Tong, Lin Guoan, Zhao Wengong, Rong Zhonghe, and Wang Fengqi to secretly operate in the Kailuan Five Mines in Luan Dong. Biao rented a house in Erdaojie, Majiagou Mine as a secret den. Zhao falsely set up a shadow garden, secretly contacting the three to plot wrongdoing. On the 14th, the Fifth Branch of the mining area detected the plot and arrested the five criminals, seizing a secret letter from Zhang with words such as going to Tianjin to recruit soldiers in order to quickly reach the required number. After interrogation, the five criminals confessed to their rebellious conspiracy. They have been sent to Tangshan for delivery to the Peiping Military Branch for trial. (16th Dispatch)

Central Political Conference

(Nanjing) The Central Political Conference held its 440th meeting on the morning of the 16th. Those in attendance included Wang Zhaoming, Ju Zheng, Ye Chucang, Chen Guofu, Lin Sen, Chu Minyi, Shi Qingyang, Zhou Qigang, Wu Jingheng, Chen Lifu, Gan Naiguang, Chen Bijun, Chuan Rulin, Chen Shuren, Tang Youren, Gu Zhenggang, Duan Xipeng and more than thirty others. Chen Guofu chaired the meeting and discussed many important cases, adjourning after 12 noon. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Central Political Conference held its 440th meeting on the morning of the 16th and resolved the following motions: (1) The proposal submitted by the Fifth Plenary Session to reduce school holidays and shorten the academic year was submitted to the Executive Yuan for discussion and reply. (2) Approval and ratification of the National Government's decree permitting Zhu Shaoliang, Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government, to resign from his concurrent post as Director of Civil Affairs, and appointing Wang Yingyu as a member of the Gansu Provincial Government and concurrently as Director of Civil Affairs. (3) Approval and ratification of the National Government's decree permitting Mao Longzhang, member of the Anhui Provincial Government and concurrently Director of Finance, to resign from his post, and appointing Yang Mianzhong as a member of the Anhui Provincial Government and concurrently as Director of Finance. (4) Approved 17 budget cases. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Tan Zhen Arrives in Nanjing from Shanghai

(Nanjing) Tan Zhen arrived in Nanjing from Shanghai on the morning of the 16th and attended the Central Political Conference immediately. According to him, his illness has not yet healed. He originally intended to go north to inspect the judiciary, but the date is undetermined. It may be possible after the spring warms up. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Wang Chonghui

Receptions After Arriving in Beijing

(Nanjing) After arriving in Beijing, Wang Chonghui went to his old residence on Tongren Street from his residence in the Mausoleum New Village at 9:00 AM on the 16th to rest and meet with old friends in Beijing. At noon, Ju Zheng, the President of the Judicial Yuan, hosted a banquet for Wang at his private residence and invited Xie Guansheng and others to accompany him. Wang is scheduled to go to Shanghai on the 18th. (16th Dispatch) (Nanjing) In order to convey central government decrees and communicate local conditions, the Guangdong military and political authorities appointed Guan Suren, Li Renren, and Deng Qingyang as permanent representatives in Beijing. Guan and Li have been appointed as legislators. Li stayed in Guangdong due to matters. He can come to Beijing next week. Guan has attended the preparatory meeting of the Legislative Yuan and has gone to Shanghai to meet Deng Qingyang, who is in Shanghai. They are scheduled to come to Beijing on the 17th to attend the first general meeting of the Legislative Yuan. Since the three committees also have the mission of liaison, in order to avoid misunderstandings from the outside, in addition to important items, they will visit the authorities at any time for contact. Ordinary events will still be conveyed by Yang Dezhao, the representative of Chen Jitang, and no other offices will be established. (16th Dispatch)

Judicial Yuan

Interprets Doubts in Civil Law

(Nanjing) The Huanggang District Court asked the Judicial Yuan to interpret various doubts regarding the abolition of adoption and the dissolution of marriage contracts. The explanation is that for the abolition of inheritance events that occur after the implementation of the Family Law of the Civil Code, since there is no law to follow, Article 1 of the General Principles of the Civil Code should be followed and the legal provisions for terminating the adoption relationship between adoptive parents and children should be adopted as a legal principle. Second, if a minor child does not agree to a marriage contract entered into by their parents on their behalf, the marriage contract is naturally invalid and there is no issue of dissolution. Instructions were given on the 16th to comply. (16th Dispatch)

He Guoguang Speaks on

Future Bandit Suppression Strategies

Consolidate Steadily and Strike Fiercely to Eliminate the Main Force of Bandits

Bandit Suppression Troops Must Cherish the People

Liu Xiang Flies to Luzhou to Address Garrison Troops

(Chongqing) He Guoguang gave a speech at a banquet held by military leaders on the 15th: (1) In the future, we must consolidate steadily and strike fiercely in order to eliminate the main force of the Communist bandits. (2) Rewards and punishments must be clear, and the various armies must coordinate their actions. (3) The hearts of the people are the prerequisite for the hearts of the military. Bandit suppression troops must cherish the people in order to win their hearts. If we win the support of the people, the hearts of the military will be solid. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Chongqing) Liu Xiang and Yang Bochang, the chief of staff of the training division, flew to Luzhou on the 16th to address the garrison troops of Fan and Zhang's brigades. They returned to Chongqing on the same day. Pan Wenhua, the division commander, led his subordinates to Luzhou by steamer on the same day to inspect the defenses and stationed there. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Chongqing) The new provincial government will be established on the 20th. He Chengjiao, who was sent by the Central Government to supervise the oath-taking, and Yang Quanyu, the new Director of Education, will fly to Chongqing on the 18th. The Chongqing Administrative Office has determined that the city library, Shuangyuan, Shizhong Building, and the new guesthouse will be used for residence. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Chongqing) Hou Zidan came to Chongqing from Songkan on the 12th to pay respects to Liu Xiang and He Guoguang and request instructions. He arrived in Chongqing on the 16th and will return to the defense area on the 23rd. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Wang Youyong, the second chief of the General Staff, took the early train on the morning of the 16th to Xun and then took a boat to Hankou. He will fly to Chongqing with Deputy Chief Li Weilun when the opportunity arises. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Yang Bandits Have a Tendency to Flee to Shaanxi

Jing Yuexiu Dispatches Heavy Troops to Block and Suppress

After Yang Monkey, a petty bandit from Yulin, crossed the river, he gathered more than 2,000 mounted bandits and is now fleeing around Daliuchang in Mongolia, showing signs of fleeing south. Jing Yuexiu has deployed heavy troops in Shenmu and the Shuangshan area of ​​Yulin to strictly block and suppress them. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch) (Tianjin) More than a hundred bandits led by Yang Monkey suddenly crossed from the border of Chahar into Wanxian County in northern Hebei on the 14th, looting and burning many villages along the way. County Magistrate Liang Weixin led more than 200 policemen to suppress them. They encountered the bandits in Huangyan Village and engaged in a two-hour fierce battle. The bandits were defeated and fled towards Shuangxian and Tangjiakou. After further pursuit, the bandits suffered heavy casualties and fled to Zijing Pass that night, reportedly entering the territory of Shanxi. (16th Dispatch)

Xiao Gan's Division Advances to Suppress the Remaining Bandits in Eastern Fujian

(Fuzhou) Xiao Gan's division is advancing in three routes to suppress the remaining bandits in eastern Fujian. Security Regiments 139 and others will be combined into one brigade under Xiao's division, with Ma Hongxing promoted to brigade commander. (16th Dispatch)

Zhang Naiyan Resigns as Envoy to Belgium

(Nanjing) Zhang Naiyan has decided to resign from his post as the ambassador to Belgium. The letter of resignation was submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday. In the future, he plans to devote himself to construction work based on what he has learned from his inspection. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Economic Commission to Hold a Standing Committee Meeting

(Nanjing) According to the Economic Commission, the administrative expenses for the 24th year of the Republic have been set at 12 million yuan, including 6 million yuan for water conservancy expenses, which is one-fifth less than last year, a reduction of 3 million yuan. It is also decided that after the three standing committee members, Chiang, Soong, and Kong, return to Beijing within days, the 12th standing committee meeting will be held to discuss and decide on the work plans for various projects this year. (16th Dispatch)

Railway in Beijing for Rent

(Nanjing) The Beijing Municipal Government intends to lease the city railway to the Jiangnan Railway Company for operation and management in order to seek development. After several rounds of discussion between the two parties, a considerable result has been achieved. It is agreed that the handover will take place on March 1 of this year. On the day of the handover, the Jiangnan Railway Company will be allowed to draw a rent of 30,000 yuan, and the rent will be 3,000 yuan per month. The lease period is set at 20 years. During the lease period, the company will use everything in good faith and maintain it properly. The scope of the lease includes all the land, tracks, houses, vehicles, and property of the Beijing Railway. However, the width of the track land is based on 31.5 English feet. The station land is rented out according to the entire original land. When the contract is officially established, personnel will be sent by both the Municipal Government and the Jiangnan Railway Company to count and hand over the items according to the list. There are also considerable regulations on the handover method when it is returned upon expiration. If the Jiangnan Railway Company intends to purchase all the assets of the city railway in the future, it can also discuss it at any time. All matters and procedures for collecting land along the line shall be handled by the company on behalf of the municipal government. The lease contract is valid for 20 years. Without the consent of the other party, neither party can terminate the contract midway. If there is a failure to comply with the regulations, the other party may demand compensation for considerable losses. If there is a possibility of renewal after the expiration, the lease may be renegotiated. (16th Dispatch)

Longhai Railway Develops Combined Water and Land Transportation

(Zhengzhou) The Longhai Railway has accumulated more than 100,000 tons of cotton in Tongguan, waiting to be shipped to Shanghai. It has now been agreed with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to actively develop combined water and land transportation, adding six ships per week to transport Shaanxi cotton exclusively. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

A Large Batch of Silver Dollars Shipped from Hong Kong to Shanghai

(Hong Kong) The eight hundred thousand yuan of silver coins purchased by the Chinese Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee were shipped to Shanghai this morning on the postal ships President Taft and Empress of Russia. The Rawleigh and Bendigo had already carried 500,000 yuan to Shanghai. The Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee purchased the silver through the Bank of China and has purchased more than one million yuan, but it was temporarily unable to load and transport it to Shanghai. Half of it will be transported to Shanghai by the President McKinley, which will arrive in Shanghai on January 21. It was learned yesterday that from now on, fast ships from Hong Kong to Shanghai will carry 500,000 yuan per ship, up to 20 million yuan. The Bank of China's active purchase of silver has become a major transaction in the Hong Kong foreign exchange market. (16th, National Dispatch)

Yellow River Silt Land Plan

(Jinan) According to a survey by the Construction Department, the water surface of the Yellow River from Rongze to Lijin is 3-4 meters higher than the ground outside the dikes, making it most suitable for siphon silt land. If 300 sets of 48-inch siphon pipes are used, 2.24 million mu of land can be silted up annually, with a revenue of 5 yuan per mu, totaling more than 12 million yuan. The project cost is agreed at 5 million yuan, and a charge of 6 jiao per mu is sufficient. The remaining clear water after siltation can increase the water volume of various rivers, and North China shipping can receive great benefits. Moreover, the German Engels plan to comprehensively treat the Yellow River in 30 years, requiring a total of 34.8 million yuan. A donation of 5 jiao per mu per year from the silted land is enough to use. (16th Dispatch)

The annual charge of 5 jiao per mu is sufficient for use. (16th Dispatch)

Hebei New Life Movement Rectifies Tianjin City Appearance

(Tianjin) The Hebei New Life Promotion Association held a meeting of executive members today to decide on measures to rectify the appearance of the city, which will be implemented immediately. (16th Dispatch)

Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce Borrows Money to Help Businesses

(Hong Kong) Business in Guangzhou has been sluggish recently, and funds are tight. The City Chamber of Commerce applied to the Department of Finance for a loan to provide relief, but the request was not approved. At 3:00 PM on the 16th, an economic design meeting was convened and it was resolved to borrow money from the Provincial Bank using real estate as collateral. (16th Central Dispatch)

Hubei Disaster Relief Association Purchases Grain for Hubei and Sells it at a Discount

(Hankou) The disaster-stricken people of Hubei are in increasing distress. The disaster-stricken people of Puqi are eating Guanyin clay to satisfy their hunger. The Provincial Disaster Relief Association has decided to purchase 100,000 dan of grain, transport it to Hubei, and sell it at a discount. (16th Dispatch)

Fujian Department of Finance Reorganizes Western Fujian Finances

(Fuzhou) The Department of Finance has decided to send personnel to western Fujian to reorganize finances and pilot legal donations and taxes. All incomes, levies, and excessive charges will be exempted in order to reduce the burden on the people after the suppression of the bandits. (16th Dispatch)

Panic Buying in Zhangzhou, Xiamen and Other Places Has Completely Subsided

(Xiamen) Panic buying subsided completely on the 16th, and all banks have returned to their original state. More than 90,000 yuan was cashed out in Zhangzhou on the 14th and 15th, and it also subsided completely on the 16th. It also subsided completely in Quanzhou on the 16th. (16th Dispatch)

He Yingqin Leaves Shanxi to Return to Peiping and Makes a Statement in Taiyuan Yesterday

Huang Fu to Fly to Beijing After Meeting He

(Taiyuan) He Yingqin and his wife took a special train on the Zhengtai Railway this afternoon, accompanied by Liu Jifei, representative of the Military Branch; Zhang Yinwu, representative of the Hebei Provincial Committee; Tao Rongbu, representative of Xi Mengsuo Wang; Liu Shifu, representative of Song Zheyuan; Liu Shuzhi, representative of Gao Guizi; and more than a dozen others, and left Taiyuan for Peiping. More than 200 people from the military, political, and other circles and representatives from all walks of life came to the station to see them off. He answered reporters' questions with a face: (1) He was very impressed with the various construction projects in Shanxi. He had not seen Director Yan for many years. Taking advantage of the opportunity to come to Shanxi, after the completion of Yan Taiweng's funeral, he spent half a day with Director Yan to express his admiration. There were no special matters that could be reported. (2) After going to Peiping, he will handle all military and political facilities in North China in accordance with the orders of the central government, and he personally has no special ideas. (3) He has not heard when Chairman Huang will go south. (4) Regarding the future crisis in the world, he believes that if the Chinese people do not unite and work hard, the country will be in danger at any time. Turning danger into safety lies only in our own efforts. (16th Dispatch)

(Peiping) Huang Fu decided to fly to Beijing after meeting He Yingqin in Peiping. The attendants and luggage are scheduled to take the train first on the evening of the 17th. The Railway Bureau has prepared a chartered car for use. There are more than 70 pieces of luggage, all of which have been sorted and parked properly. Those traveling with him include Xu Xiuzhi and Zhao Shuyong. It is rumored that Huang plans to stay in Tianjin for one night when he passes through Tianjin to entertain foreign guests. Tianjin is arranging accommodation on behalf of him. Yin Tong and Li Ze are traveling to Tianjin on the same train. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Peiping) According to railway information, He Yingqin will arrive at Shijiazhuang at 7:30 PM on the 16th, stay briefly, and then take the Pinghan train back north. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch) (Peiping) Taiyuan telegram, He Yingqin took a train from Taiyuan at noon to Peiping and is expected to arrive in Peiping tomorrow morning. (16th Dispatch)

(Peiping) Sun Lianzhong went to Tianjin to wish his mother a happy birthday and will come to Peiping tonight to pay his respects to He Yingqin and return the visits of various dignitaries who came to offer congratulations. (16th Dispatch)

(Peiping) Yu Xuezhong is scheduled to come to Peiping tomorrow afternoon to visit He Yingqin. (16th Dispatch)

(Peiping) According to the Military Branch, He Yingqin left on the afternoon of the 16th to return to Peiping and will arrive at 7:00 AM on the 17th. The Jurentang residence has been cleaned yesterday. At that time, representatives of various agencies and senior officers of the Military Branch will go to the station to welcome him. (16th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(C) For advertisements in the news column, each line is 40 characters high, with a minimum of three lines, priced at $0.90 per line per day. First Class (A) Half-page position next to the newspaper title on the cover, priced at $225 per page per day. (B) From the bottom cover to before the telecommunications news, each holding is calculated as 82 characters high, with a minimum of two holdings, priced at $1.80 per line per day.

Second Class Advertisements in the summary classification area, each line is 20 characters long, with a minimum of four lines each time, priced at $0.40 per line per day. Third Class (A) Advertisements in the local supplement news column, each line is 40 characters high, with a minimum of three lines each time, priced at $0.60 per line per day. (B) Advertisements in the local supplement classified advertisement area, each line is 20 characters high, with a minimum of four lines each time, priced at $0.25 per line per day.

Current Commentary: Difficulties in the Textile Industry and the Issue of Raw Cotton Taxation

Since it was reported that a certain Central Committee member advocated saving the nation's yarn factories, the clamor about how difficult the textile industry is has become quite noisy again. As commercial customs coincide with the time of year-end settlement, some domestic factories with slightly weaker financial strength are indeed in a state of suspension and reorganization due to the impact of the sluggish market. Even yarn factories with relatively strong strength on weekdays inevitably suffer from the pain of cheap yarn and expensive cotton. Coupled with the decline of the national economy in recent years, the difficulties have deepened day by day. Under this situation, how will the national textile industry tide over this difficulty? It is indeed worthy of our deep consideration.

After silently observing the various statements made by all parties to rescue the yarn industry in recent days, it seems that their sights are all focused on the single point of cheap yarn and expensive cotton, believing that it is useless unless the value of raw cotton (i.e., the cost of raw materials) is reduced. The intention of promoting this statement is probably that the price of standard yarn has fallen to more than 180 yuan, while the price of raw cotton has become increasingly expensive due to hoarding and manipulation. As a result, the cost of each piece of yarn far exceeds the price of the yarn. In order to suppress the price of cotton, there is a saying that the current import tariff on raw cotton should be reduced. It seems reasonable to say this, but as far as I know, the expensiveness of cotton is not the fundamental difficulty of the yarn industry, and it is even more doubtful whether reducing the import tariff on raw cotton can immediately achieve the effect of cheap cotton. My country is known as an agricultural country, although cotton production cannot completely meet demand. However, under the slogan of national recovery and the revitalization of rural areas in recent years, the cotton planting industry seems to have become the main agricultural investment of the banking industry. The gradual progress of cotton production towards a bumper harvest is indeed a very obvious benefit and cannot be denied as a great thing. Because it is the phenomenon that should occur after the revitalization of rural areas. Moreover, what cannot be ignored is that since the current tariff rules were promulgated in July 1934, the import tax rate on raw cotton has been 5 gold units per 100 kilograms, which is 43% heavier than the originally set tariff rule of 3.5 gold units. At that time, people in the country generally believed that foreign factories, such as Japanese merchants, which consumed the most foreign cotton in the country, would inevitably suffer a great blow. Chinese factories could take advantage of this opportunity to compete favorably. This is why Japanese factories expressed their opposition to the increase in tariffs on raw cotton. Although this matter has passed, if our people today advocate increasing the import of foreign cotton for the sake of temporary interests and in order to suppress domestic cotton, I am afraid that the final result will only be laughed at by foreign merchants. If it is said that the price of cotton can be lowered as a result, it is very unlikely. It must be known that the current trend of cotton prices towards expensiveness is due to the impact of the severe drought in the United States last year and is completely based on the principle of supply and demand changes in the international market, which cannot be manipulated by the tariff rules of a single country.

Furthermore, I must fully recognize the fundamental difficulties of yarn factories today, which are nothing more than the backwardness of production efficiency and the oppression of foreign capital. The former belongs to the issue of production costs, while the latter is the market protection policy of a so-called independent country, which cannot be ignored. If you want to revitalize the domestic textile industry at this time of increasing global competition, I am afraid that there is no other special and effective plan besides this fundamental rescue method. If you only know how to solve problems from the trivial matters, it will not only have the suspicion of going back and forth, but it is also not the original intention of the Chinese people to seek self-salvation.

International Press Corps Departs for Jiangxi

(Nanjing) The international press corps, a group of twenty-six individuals heading to Jiangxi, departed from Nanjing on the Jiangshun and Datong steamers in the morning and afternoon of the 16th. Twenty-one people were on the Jiangshun steamer, accompanied by Huang Chaoqin, section chief of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Huang Renlin from the Lixingshe, departing at 8:00 AM. Five people were on the Datong steamer, heading west at 6:00 PM. They will gather in Xunyang and then proceed to Nanchang to inspect various locations according to the planned route. They are expected to return to Shanghai around the 29th. (16th Central News Agency dispatch)

League of Nations Administrative Council Postpones Saar Issue Meeting, Causing Complications

Germany Demands Stipulation of Transfer Date

League of Nations in a Dilemma, Seeking Compromise

(Geneva) According to informed sources, Britain and France requested that the Saar be designated as part of the demilitarized Rhineland, leading to the postponement of the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting originally scheduled for today to transfer the Saar to Germany. The Administrative Council announced that many issues concerning the Saar would be resolved during this session, rather than leaving detailed procedures to be handled by a committee. The German side has not expressed any reaction to this new development. It is rumored that any delay will cause resentment throughout Germany, as the German government and people are united in their firm demand for the immediate return of the Saar to the fatherland. Moreover, Germany's demand was resolute even before the vote. Now that the results of the vote have been revealed, with a strong majority of over 90% in favor of returning to Germany, there is no room for further delay in returning the lost territory. Therefore, the demands of Britain and France have placed the League of Nations Administrative Council in a dilemma, as the League wants to resolve the Saar issue immediately without creating unnecessary complications. However, with these demands from the two major powers in the League, the Administrative Council can only follow Britain and France's lead. Since the final resolution of the Saar issue will be delayed, various countries must engage in off-session consultations to reach a compromise acceptable to all parties. (16th National Telegram)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council held an important meeting this afternoon to consider the report of the Saar plebiscite commission and postponed making a decision on handing over the Saar to Germany. People in Geneva speculated about the reasons for the temporary postponement. Some sources said that this move was related to the desire expressed by political circles this morning for a generous handover of the Saar, or that technical arrangements had encountered setbacks. However, this postponement will not last long. It is rumored that the Administrative Council may convene again tomorrow. Meanwhile, according to news from Berlin, the German government has made a strong demand to the League of Nations, requesting a fixed date for the return of the Saar and the withdrawal of the international troops stationed there. However, according to official sources, the German Consul General in Geneva, Mr. Krull, did not make any demands when he met with Baron Aloisi today, but made it clear that the Saar should be returned as soon as possible so that the German government could take over the area within a month. Germany now feels that there is no reason to delay the handover, and Germany is now in a position to insist on its rights without having to ask anyone for concessions. (16th Reuters dispatch)

Continued telegram: According to responsible sources, the reason for the Administrative Council's postponement of the decision to hand over the Saar was due to France's raising of the issue of the demilitarization of the Saar. According to Articles 42 to 44 of the Treaty of Versailles, all German territory on the left bank of the Rhine must be demilitarized. France is now demanding the demolition of railways related to military use and the facilities for loading and unloading troop trains. (16th Reuters dispatch)

(London) British sources claim that even with the abolition of the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles, the Saar must be a non-militarized zone. (16th National Telegram)

(Geneva) Various parties are currently conducting talks outside the League of Nations Administrative Council regarding the Saar issue, to find a solution that is satisfactory to both France and Germany. The point of divergence between France and Germany lies in the demilitarization of the Saar region. France believes that the Treaty of Versailles stipulates that the demilitarized zone on the left bank of the Rhine should include the Saar, and that this issue did not need to be raised before the plebiscite decided the fate of the Saar. However, Germany believes that after the plebiscite resulted in a German victory, the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles regarding the Saar region no longer have any reason to exist. It is generally believed that this can still be resolved smoothly. Diplomatic talks between various countries are now continuing. This morning, Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov met with Polish Foreign Minister Beck to discuss the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. Beck is still ill. French Foreign Minister Laval will visit Beck this afternoon. The discussions will cover all aspects of French-Polish relations, the Eastern European Pact, and the Rome agreements between Italy and France. People are very interested in these matters. In addition, Yugoslav Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Jevtić will arrive here soon, and British Foreign Secretary Simon will also return here. (16th Havas dispatch)

(London) The British government now advocates for a prompt decision on the timing of the League of Nations Saar Governing Commission's handover of the Saar administration to the German authorities, and also advocates for the prompt withdrawal of the international gendarmerie. The British government's views will be expressed by Foreign Secretary Simon at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting. Simon may depart for Geneva tomorrow or Friday. The customs checkpoints currently existing between the Saar and various parts of Germany will be removed. It is currently expected that similar customs checkpoints will be established between the Saar and France, and that arrangements will be made to allow the people of the Saar to exchange francs for German currency. Informed circles in London believe that the clauses in the Treaty of Versailles regarding Germany's demilitarization will naturally apply to the Saar, as the Saar is now part of German territory. France now believes that the result of this vote will strengthen Hitler's position domestically and may further increase the decisiveness of diplomatic affairs. It is feared that the Austrian National Socialist Party will therefore attempt to revive its activities. The Times says that the overall situation should now be handled with extreme caution, and that France, Britain, and Italy should work together to deal with Hitlerized Germany. (16th Reuters dispatch)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council is scheduled to hold a closed-door meeting at 4:00 PM today, followed by a formal meeting. The formal meeting will receive the results of the Saar vote and the report of Mr. Weede, Chairman of the Saar Plebiscite Commission. Then, League of Nations President Rüsthi will invite Aloisi to speak. Aloisi will propose that the entire Saar region be returned to Germany immediately. (16th National Telegram)

Ballots Arrive in Geneva

(Geneva) All members of the Saar plebiscite commission, carrying dozens of boxes of ballots, departed from Saarbrücken by special train yesterday and arrived here this afternoon. Senior officials of the League of Nations and representatives of the international press welcomed them, and a large contingent of police was dispatched to protect them. The destruction of these ballots will be decided by the Administrative Council. As for the recount of the ballots, it is generally believed that since such a large majority voted in favor of returning to Germany, there is no need for a recount. (16th Havas dispatch)

Saar Restores to Normal

(Saarbrücken) The scenery here has returned to normal, but flags can still be seen flying everywhere. The offices of the plebiscite commission and the Saar administrative commission are very quiet, in stark contrast to the lively state of a few days ago. The chairman of the administrative commission, Mr. Knox, went to Geneva by car this morning to inform the League of Nations Administrative Council that the sooner the Saar region is transferred, the better. In the eyes of the residents of the Saar, the authority of the administrative commission has almost been lost due to the results of the plebiscite. If public security is threatened, it will be difficult for the administrative commission to take serious decisions. It is generally believed that Knox will advocate that the transfer of sovereignty should take place on March 1, rather than between March 15 and April 1. Currently, the resettlement movement of anti-National Socialist Saar residents continues, with approximately one thousand people requesting protection from the French consulate every day. Newspapers that support maintaining the status quo have now ceased publication. (16th Havas dispatch)

Germans Celebrate Wildly All Night

Torchlight Processions Stretch for Miles

Party and National Anthems and Saar Song Harmonize; Mourning Clothes and Coffins Mock the Status Quo

Saarbrücken: The National Socialist Party won a large majority in this vote. Germany and the Saar are both celebrating greatly. All streets in the Saar were decorated with lanterns last night. Tens of thousands of men, women, and children marched through the city holding Chinese lanterns. The processions stretched for miles, and crowds of onlookers watched. When the lantern parades passed, there were cheers, as if everyone was crazy. In addition, there were dozens of military bands and other musical groups gathered in the streets, playing patriotic marches, the German national anthem, party songs, and the Saar song, showing their joy. Shouts of "Long live" rose and fell, never ceasing. A group of young people, dressed in mourning clothes, wearing tall hats, carried a coffin with the inscription "Mr. Bureau is dead" and paraded through the city. The crowds who saw it laughed and cheered wildly. A wreath with the words "You have won" was placed in front of the offices of the labor newspaper, which had predicted that the anti-Hitler faction would win. Such humorous events were too numerous to record. Fortunately, those who were targeted endured it and no incidents occurred. (15th Reuters dispatch)

Saarbrücken: The results of the Saar vote have been announced. The celebration that the National Socialist Party called "the festival of the century" was held in the evening. The enthusiasm of the people marching with torches cannot be described in words. At 6:00 PM, a continuous stream of people were marching, perhaps as many as 200,000. Observations indicate that this number is accurate and not an exaggeration, as the crowds marched for three hours without ceasing. Stormtroopers with motorcycles and sidecar motorcycles led the way, all covered with swastika flags. There were also people carrying effigies representing those who wanted to maintain the status quo, and the crowds clapped and cheered to mock them. Military bands played the Saar song, interspersed with the German national anthem and the National Socialist Party anthem. As dusk fell, the whole city was illuminated by electric lights, and almost every house had a huge image of Hitler, up to one meter high. However, the fervent emotions of the National Socialist Party quickly faded. By 10:00 PM, most of those who participated in the celebration, tired from a day of rushing around, had quietly returned home. (15th Havas dispatch)

Overseas Chinese Celebrate Victory

(Qingdao) German residents in this city hung flags on the 16th to celebrate the Saar vote victory. (16th special dispatch)

Buenos Aires, Argentina: The government has recently allowed German residents here to fly the German flag to celebrate the return of the Saar region to Germany. (15th Havas dispatch)

(Berlin) Germany held large-scale demonstrations across the country to celebrate the victory of the Saar vote. Propaganda Minister Goebbels spoke in Berlin, denouncing the Treaty of Versailles, saying that it was "meaningless and contrary to nature." He also criticized the Saar Administrative Commission, and finally suggested to the Saar socialist leader Planck that he might as well dig a grave and bury all the German exiles abroad in it. In conclusion, he said, "German territory is now complete and intact. Let us unite and move forward." (15th Havas dispatch)

Safety of the Opposition is Uncertain

Saarbrücken: Amid this unforgettable joy, many people quietly packed their bags and paid attention to the train schedules. These are Saarlanders who oppose Hitlerism and fear that they will inevitably suffer under Hitler's rule, so they are planning to move to a better place. It is said that at least six or seven prominent figures from the Socialist Party and the Communist Party have already crossed the border. (10th Reuters dispatch)

Saarbrücken: So far, there have only been some minor incidents in various places, all of which are insignificant. For example, the headquarters of the Socialist Party was surrounded by members of the German Front who wanted to break into the headquarters. The authorities closed the headquarters to avoid conflict. National Socialist Party members have repeatedly invaded private homes. In several places, the police have voluntarily abandoned their posts and been replaced by National Socialist Party members in uniform. (15th Lewas dispatch)

Saarbrücken: After the results of the plebiscite were announced, the authorities took preventive measures, ordering all personnel in anti-National Socialist organizations to withdraw. As a result, the "People's Voice News" and the "Workers' Welfare Group" and other major strongholds of the anti-Hitler faction have been dismantled and seem to be on the verge of extinction. No overstepping actions occurred when the anti-National Socialist organizations were dismantled, perhaps due to fear of the international police. However, it can be said that it is a double misfortune that the outcome of the vote to maintain the status quo has failed, and personal safety is also a concern. Moreover, after the announcement of the plebiscite results, the international organizations seemed to think that their mission had been completed. For example, the leader of the Catholic anti-Hitler faction, Mr. Hoffmann, fearing for his life, requested protection from Captain Hannesse, an Englishman and police inspector of the Saar, but to no avail. He had no choice but to seek protection from others until he left the Saar region last night. In addition, fifteen French families were forced to leave their homes due to threats from the National Socialist Party and are temporarily sheltering around the mines managed by France. In view of these various incidents, people on the anti-National Socialist Party side expected the League of Nations to notify the international authorities that they are still responsible for maintaining order in the Saar region. However, some of the most prestigious leaders of the National Socialist Party announced to the representatives of Havas News Agency that the policy the party intends to continue to adopt in the Saar region now shows a tendency to ease. This policy can be divided into the following four points: (1) The National Socialist Party's victory on the Saar issue will not harm relations between France and Germany, because after the Saar issue is resolved, there will be no more territorial issues between France and Germany. (2) Regarding the leaders of the anti-National Socialist Party, the National Socialist Party believes that these people should be aware that their position is very difficult. (3) The National Socialist Party intends to use persuasion to convince opposition party members. (4) From a religious point of view, the result of this Saar vote can provide some relevant negotiating elements for the relationship between Germany and the Roman Curia, because German Catholics know that Germany and the Curia have the possibility of closer cooperation. Now that Saar Catholics have expressed their support for Hitler, it can further inspire German Catholics. (16th Havas dispatch)

Streets Renamed to Commemorate

(Berlin) The municipal authorities announced that Stresemann Street would be renamed "Saar Street" to commemorate January 13. This thoroughfare connects two stations, and trains can go directly from that station to the Saar, so this street was specially selected as Saar Street to show victory and to remember. The renaming ceremony was personally held by the Mayor of Berlin. (15th National News Agency dispatch)

Reactions from Various Countries

Italian Officials Satisfied

(Rome) Italian official circles unanimously expressed open satisfaction with the enthusiasm of the Saar people to return to their homeland. They also believe that since the number of votes for merging with Germany is so large, a completely clear situation has been created, and there is no objection. The League of Nations' handling of this issue must also follow a certain path, without much worry. (15th National News Agency dispatch)

Austrian People Rejoice

(Vienna) When the people of Austria heard the results of the Saar vote, all those with nationalistic ideas were overjoyed. However, the government authorities are making every effort to prevent the expression of public sentiment, and have banned newspapers in Vienna from publishing extras or holding demonstrations. However, after receiving the news of the voting results in major cities in the provinces, the people spontaneously gathered in the streets, shouting slogans such as "Long live Germany" and "Long live the Saar" to celebrate. In the afternoon, the newspapers published detailed telegrams from the Saar, Berlin, and Geneva on a large scale. When they were sold on the streets, they were sold out in an instant. The Vienna Daily also raised in its editorial that former French Prime Minister Clemenceau claimed that there were 150,000 French people in the Saar region. Now the French people have been eliminated, and only 2,000 remain. Clemenceau advocated the annexation of the Saar by France during his lifetime. (19th National Telegram)

(Vienna) Adam, the director of the Federal Propaganda Committee and the commander of the patriotic special forces, recently gave a radio broadcast speech, saying that in this Saar plebiscite, 90% supported returning to Germany. This is not only the wish of the National Socialist Party, but also the wish of other parties. However, what these people support is Germany, not the Germany led by the National Socialist Party. He also said, "Germany's victory in the Saar vote and the realization of the hopes of the German nation is something we should be happy about. Our Austrian concept of Germany is completely separate from our opinion of political parties and is not confused at all. Austria is a free German state. Austria has its own point of view and does not want to mix it up with Germany and those who are temporarily in power in Germany." (16th Havas dispatch)

Editorials of Various Newspapers

French-German Cooperation Builds a Bridge

(Berlin) Today's newspapers, after expressing their pleasure at the results of the Saar vote, all quoted Hitler's words, saying that "after the Saar returns to Germany, the territorial dispute between France and Germany will completely disappear." Propaganda Minister Goebbels also said in his speech that "cooperation between the two major neighboring nations has now built a bridge of transition. We may be in a historical period of transformation in European politics today, which should be attributed to Germany's decisive policy, and only Hitler can represent it." (15th Havas dispatch)

Russia Worries About Germany's Eastward Ambitions (Moscow) Soviet informed sources expressed surprise at the fact that the pro-German annexation faction won an overwhelming majority in the Saar plebiscite. However, it is said that the Saar vote achieved this result due to the National Socialist Party's vigorous propaganda and the Saar people's patriotic concepts. In addition, Soviet people also share the same views as people in other countries, believing that the clear voting results have clarified the situation in Western Europe, especially the relationship between France and Germany. It is generally believed that Hitler may soon make more concrete proposals to establish French-German understanding. However, it is particularly worrying that Germany's authority has increased after the Saar vote and that it may make risky and opportunistic moves in the weaker areas of the Central European political front. (15th Havas dispatch)

Social Morality Should Be Respected: The Vatican newspaper "L'Osservatore Romano" commented on the results of the Saar vote, hoping that a social and moral reaction would occur immediately to benefit the broad cause of peace. However, it is uncertain whether there will be brutal acts of revenge in the Saar region afterwards. (15th Havas dispatch)

Zinoviev Assassination Case: Zinoviev and Others Formally Tried

Discovery of the So-Called [Moscow Center Group]

Engaged in Secret Anti-Soviet Activities

(Moscow) During the investigation of the Ningrad secret counter-revolutionary group related to the murder of Kirov, new information about the secret counter-revolutionary activities of Zinoviev, Gahev, and others has been discovered. At the same time, Bakayev and Shavrov confessed to various facts about the recent secret activities of the counter-revolutionary group [Moscow Center Group] during the investigation. Therefore, Zinoviev, Yevdokimov, Kamenev, Fedorov and fifteen others have been handed over to the Military Tribunal of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union for trial. The case began today in Leningrad. (TASS dispatch on the 15th)

(Moscow) The indictment of the case against Zinoviev, Kamenev, and others has been released here as follows: During the investigation of the secret counter-revolutionary terrorist group that murdered Kirov, it was proven that the so-called [Moscow Center Group] was formed by former leaders of the Zinoviev anti-Soviet faction. Although the faction had surrendered, their secret work did not stop. Their purpose was to realize their counter-revolutionary attempts in accordance with the so-called Zinoviev-Trotsky program, and to carry out secret counter-revolutionary work in Moscow. It has now been proven that the members of the so-called [Moscow Center Group] are Zinoviev, Yevdokimov, Gherdik, Bakayev, Kuklin, Kamenev, Shavrov, Fedorov, and Gorshin. They also organized active members of the former Zinoviev anti-Soviet faction around them, while maintaining regular contact with members of the Leningrad group (i.e., those sentenced by the Military Tribunal of the Supreme Court on December 28 and 29, 1934). According to Fedorov's own confession, the "Moscow Center Group" was the political center that directed party members in Moscow and Leningrad for many years. One of the main purposes of this secret counter-revolutionary group led by the "Moscow Center Group" was to preserve its "cadres", accumulate its strength, and increase the hatred of its members for the leaders of the party and the Soviet government. They spread distorted reports of facts about domestic and foreign events among their members and made public counter-revolutionary explanations, etc. These counter-revolutionary "reports" were spread by those closest to Zinoviev and Yevdokimov, and Zinoviev and Yevdokimov used their political positions to carry out their criminal purposes. The trial proved that members of the "Moscow Center Group" such as Kuklin, Gherdik, Yevdokimov, and Sharov acted in this way. They frequently went to Leningrad and maintained counter-revolutionary contact with members of the "Leningrad Center Group." According to Fedorov's confession, this secret counter-revolutionary group never hesitated to use any means when it fought against the Soviet government. In this poisonous atmosphere of Zinoviev's secret group, the development and strengthening of fascist struggle methods and open terror psychology were not accidental, and as a result, the assassination of Kirov occurred. The defendants in this case and those in the case that needs to be further investigated all said that this tendency was the inevitable result of the entire nature and content of Zinoviev's secret work, and it was unavoidable. Defendant Zhelkov also said so, and said that Nikolaev's assassination methods were directly related to this "extreme tendency," and he said that the latter was based on Zinoviev's counter-revolutionary attempt. Defendant Bashkirov also said, "Nikolaev's assassination was precisely because he was a member of the Trotsky-Zinoviev counter-revolutionary organization and was educated by it, so the entire Trotsky-Zinoviev counter-revolutionary organization should be responsible for this." The trial did not prove that the "Moscow Center Group" had approved or instructed the assassination of Kirov, but in terms of the atmosphere and nature of the "Moscow Center Group," they must have known that the members of the group had a tendency toward terrorism, and even incited this tendency. The members of the "Moscow Center Group," especially Zinoviev, Yevdokimov, Gherdik, and Kamenev, must bear full moral and political responsibility. Not only that, according to Soviet law, they must also be responsible for the results of their own counter-revolutionary actions (that is, forcing their Leningrad group to take the path of terrorist actions). The defendants themselves cannot deny this responsibility, at least morally and politically.

When defendant Zinoviev spoke about his responsibility for the murder on December 1, he said, "The objective development of the situation is like this, and I can only plead guilty. If the anti-Party movement in Leningrad was so sharp in the past few years, it cannot but promote the degeneration of these revolutionaries. This assassination casts such an incomprehensible light on the entire anti-Party movement in the past. Therefore, I admit that it is correct to say that the former Zinoviev anti-Party organization should bear political responsibility for the assassination of Kirov."

Other defendants related to this case who have been tried, such as Bakayev, Gorshin, Fedorov, Yevdokimov, Sharov, Kuklin, and Gherdik, all admitted to being members of the "Moscow Center Group." Gerson, Panlemov, Brav, Herzberg, Vavilovitch, and Sakhov, etc., admitted to participating in the Zinoviev counter-revolutionary group. Zhelkov, Anishi, Bashkirov, and Terasov, etc., admitted that they participated in the Leningrad Zinoviev counter-revolutionary group.

Kamenev admitted his guilt and said that until 1932, he had participated in secret counter-revolutionary activities and had been a member of the "Moscow Center Group," but he had not completely severed relations with Zinoviev, only because of some daily life conditions. Kamenev also admitted that he "failed to actively and forcefully fight against the phenomenon of degeneration, which was the result of the anti-Party movement, and based on this, the dregs of the former anti-Party group were able to produce bandits, and at the same time, they were able to realize their criminal actions."

Zinoviev admitted his guilt and confirmed the existence of the Zinoviev faction center, and he did participate in it. Based on the above, the crimes committed by the nineteen defendants are as follows: Most of them participated in the secret counter-revolutionary group "Moscow Center Group," and the rest actively participated in the activities of secret counter-revolutionary groups in Moscow and Leningrad, resulting in the assassination of Kirov. In other words, they committed the crimes listed in Article 17 and Article 58, Sections 8 and 11 of the Criminal Law. (TASS dispatch on the 15th)

Opening of the 16th Soviet Congress

Commemorating Kirov and Praising Stalin

(Moscow) The 16th Soviet Congress of the Russian Socialist Federative Soviet Republic opened today in Moscow. Attendees included representatives from the 23 provinces and states, 14 autonomous republics, and 12 autonomous regions that make up the state. The agenda of the Congress includes the government work report by Sulemov, Chairman of the Council of People's Commissars of the Russian Soviet Republic, the urban economy report by the Minister of Urban Economy, the health work report by the Minister of Health, the report on the economic and cultural construction of the Tatar Autonomous Republic by the Chairman of the Central Executive Committee of the Republic, the report on constitutional issues, and the election of the next members of the Central Executive Committee of the Russian Soviet Republic and the representatives of the Russian Soviet Republic to the Soviet National Committee. The Congress opened with an opening speech by Kalinin, Chairman of the Central Executive Committee, and Stalin, Molotov, Kalinin, Kaganovich, Voroshilov, and Sulemov were elected as the presidium. Many members of the diplomatic corps and foreign journalists attended. The Soviet Congresses of Ukraine and Transcaucasia also opened today. (TASS dispatch on the 15th)

(Moscow) Kalinin, Chairman of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, gave an opening speech at the 16th Soviet Congress of the Russian Soviet Republic, commemorating the murder of the great genius Kirov, who devoted his life to the people of the Soviet Union. The delegates to the Congress all stood up to mourn Kirov. Kalinin also said that since the last Congress, all the people of the Russian Republic have worked hard, and the results are very satisfactory. He listed the great buildings of various economic sectors, which have all started manufacturing in recent years. He also said that the collectivization of agriculture has almost been completed, and pointed out the great labor, which has now achieved the result of abolishing the bread ration system. "All the great work that has been completed, its promoter, inspirer, and organizer is Stalin." At this time, the Congress gave Stalin a long cheer, and all the delegates stood up and gave Stalin a long applause, with a sound like thunder. (TASS dispatch on the 16th)

British University Students Organize Tibetan Expedition

(London) Cambridge University graduate Cobbick, who traveled two thousand miles in Tibet two years ago, all in places never before reached by Europeans, has recently organized a new expedition, which is about to depart. It is planned to enter western China from Myanmar and then to Tibet. Cobbick is currently waiting for permission from the Chinese government and is in close contact with Guo Taiqi, the Chinese envoy to Britain, and the Indian Affairs Department. The expedition members will leave Britain no later than mid-February. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

French Authorities Delay Trip to London

Disarmament Stance Awaiting Study

Anglo-French Talks to Begin Next Month

(Paris) French Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval, who were originally scheduled to go to London around January 20, have now been delayed and are scheduled to depart for Britain on January 31. This date was decided this morning when Flandin met with British Ambassador to France Clerk. The Anglo-French talks will mainly focus on discussing the issue of disarmament. The British government hopes that Germany will rejoin the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference, but so far, French Foreign Minister Laval has focused on studying various international issues, and has not yet determined France's position on disarmament. Moreover, it is impossible for Laval to do so before consulting with his cabinet members. Therefore, he had to postpone the date of his trip to Britain until the end of the month. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

(London) Although the situation in Europe has become slightly clearer due to the end of the Saar plebiscite, it has now suddenly become dim again, because the visit to London by French Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval has been delayed. This news, which was transmitted to the diplomatic community after the cabinet meeting on Monday, seems to have confirmed the claim that obstacles have arisen in the Anglo-French talks. According to reliable sources, the two French politicians were originally scheduled to come here next week, but now they will be delayed until January 31. However, according to non-official sources, it may be postponed indefinitely. It is rumored here that Foreign Secretary Simon reported the situation of his talks with Laval in Geneva last Saturday at the cabinet meeting. As a result, the cabinet agreed that the meeting should be postponed. It is also widely rumored here that Laval means that France will not agree to cancel the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles without British security guarantees, but the British side is still unable to agree to this guarantee. (National dispatch on the 15th)

(London) Official sources believe that Britain will propose to hold talks separately with representatives of European countries, and the first to be held will be the talks between Britain and France. Political figures attach great importance to the attitude of French public opinion towards the results of the Saar plebiscite, believing that it is evidence of France's desire for reconciliation, and this desire coincides with what Hitler expressed in his speech today. As for the speech delivered by French Prime Minister Flandin after the Saar plebiscite was announced, it was especially praised by those in charge here. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

(London) The British League of Nations Union shares the same attitude as the British authorities, firmly insisting on finding ways to allow Germany to return to Geneva, and the full results of the Rome Accords in terms of military arrangements are more well-founded. The Union issued a comment on the results of the Saar plebiscite, saying, "On the whole, it is quite interesting to observe the impact of the results of the Saar plebiscite on Hitler's foreign policy. Does Hitler feel that the time has come and should resolutely move towards the path of understanding with France? It is too early to predict this at present, but Germany can no longer use delaying tactics in the future to refuse to cooperate and engage in easing the European situation. In short, the Saar plebiscite has a very important result, that is, whether the peaceful aspirations touted by the Third Reich are sincere, and this will be proved by facts in the future." (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

France Responds to German Government on Eastern European Pact Issue

(Berlin) Regarding the issue of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, the late French Foreign Minister Barthou went to London in early July last year to discuss it and obtained British approval. The British government notified the relevant countries to seek their consent. The German government issued a memorandum on September 10, raising reservations, saying that Germany would rather support bilateral treaties, but does not oppose multilateral treaties. However, when concluding multilateral treaties, the relevant countries should consult each other to seek a solution, and it should not be stipulated that military assistance must be provided to each other in the event of war. France has recently issued a response to this memorandum, which will be delivered to Foreign Secretary Bulow by Ambassador to Germany Ponsart. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Roosevelt Will Send Message to Senate

Advocates Joining World Court and the Case is Expected to Pass

(Washington) According to sources at the White House today, President Roosevelt will send a message to the Senate tomorrow, advocating that the United States join the World Court. The content of the message will be largely the same as Senator Robinson's speech when the Senate began debating the World Court case. According to Robinson's reason, the World Court handles international events with law instead of anarchy, and the United States' participation does not involve other disputes, nor does it need to abandon its traditional policies, but only expresses the sincerity of the American people's cooperation. As for the Senate's debate on this case, government leaders today advocated that it be extended indefinitely, but some senators predicted that they will express it at the end of this week. According to supporters' estimates, the case can get 69 votes, exceeding one-third. Opponents such as Borah and Norris also admit that it can be passed at this time, but they hope to win more opposition votes during the debate. (National

dispatch)

Four British Airships Depart for Singapore

(London) Four airships of the 205th Airship Squadron stationed in Singapore, which have been reassembled here, departed today from the Pemblok Dockyard and flew to the Singapore naval base, 8,000 miles away. U.S. Inflationary Leaders Convene

National Financial Conference

(Washington) Inflationary leader Thomas announced today that ten groups representing half of the nation's people will attend the financial conference when it convenes on Wednesday. The conference was convened by Thomas and aims to draft an American monetary system plan based on the following points: (1) Cheap currency, (2) the limit of currency devaluation, which will probably be based on the 1926 parity, (3) to recommend to Congress the methods to complete this matter, (4) government management of banks, etc. Participants in the financial conference include the American Military Encirclement, the Coin League, the American Monetary Reform Association, the National Savings Association, the Western Silver Association, and the American Social Justice Group, etc. In addition, there are various agricultural organizations. These organizations are very influential in financial issues and have the common goal of raising agricultural product prices, but they lack unity on the silver issue. (National dispatch on the 15th)

Research on the Appearance of a Nova in the Northern Hercules Constellation

(Nanjing) In mid-December last year, British amateur astronomer Brown discovered a nova in the Northern Hercules constellation. According to the Central Astronomical Observatory, the star is actually the Nova Hercules, which belongs to a type of variable star. The nova discovered this time is the Star of Bethlehem mentioned in the Bible, which appeared once at the time of Jesus' birth. Its position is about ten degrees northwest of Vega. The brightness of the star is now gradually decreasing. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 16th)

International High Industry Telegraphic News

January 16th Reuters Special Business Telegraph

Gold and Silver: London gold price today is 141 shillings and 6 pence, down 10 pence from yesterday. London silver price unchanged today, spot price remains 24 and 5625/10000 pence, futures 24 and 6875/10000 pence. Speculators are both buying and selling, and there are some transactions when the market is stable.

Exchange Rates: British-American: The London foreign exchange market experienced severe price fluctuations this morning, which greatly affected trading. The opening price for British-American exchange was $4.8725, up 375 from yesterday's US-British closing. It then fell to $4.86375, and then rose again. The latest price is $4.879375, up 6875 from the opening price.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs 31, down 59 points from yesterday. Afterwards, it fluctuated. At 2 PM, the price was 74 francs 28, down 3 points from the opening.

American-British: The volatility of yesterday's New York foreign exchange market has not subsided today. The opening price for American-British exchange was $4.875, up 625 from yesterday. Within an hour of opening, this price did not change much. The opening price for American-French exchange was $6.57125, down 875.

Cotton and Wheat: American Cotton: The cotton market opened lower by about 3 points due to sales by spot traders. Buyers were still from the same industry. After the price fell, the downward trend subsided slightly.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened slightly higher and showed signs of rising due to better foreign prices and unfavorable weather reports. According to weather forecasts, the weather will be colder, with rain and snow.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market responded to yesterday's sharp fall in US wheat prices this morning. At 1 PM, the May futures price was 4 shillings and 11.25 pence, down 1 pence.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market experienced a severe decline today. At 1 PM, the May futures price was 679, down 6 points from the previous closing price.

Rubber: London: The rubber market was calm today. The transaction price for April/June futures at noon was 6.625 pence, down 0.0625.

New York: Rubber futures opened about 20 points higher. Securities: New York: Before the opening of the securities market, a factor favorable to the market was the possibility of an early recovery in securities prices. Brokers also do not expect prices to fall, as commercial news remains good and speculative buying is now in a more stable position, because most of the weaker bulls have been eliminated. A factor unfavorable to the market is the uncertainty of the gold bar issue, which may continue to dominate the market in the near future. The stock market opened slightly active this morning, and the market was stable. Most stocks rose slightly. Case Threshing Machine rose 1 point, while Columbia Gas & Electric fell 1 point. The market is expected to rebound, which is expected, as there were many sales during the gold standard panic. It is reported that rubber consumption figures are better than expected. Oil production last week averaged 2,537,000 barrels per day, up 149,000 barrels from the previous week. Electricity production is higher than the previous week, and the steel industry is also expected to increase production. All of these are good commercial news. Li Benwei Writes a Letter Stating the Distress of Remarrying

(Beiping) Li Benwei, the concubine of Li Yuanhong, recently remarried Wang Kuixuan in Qingdao. Li is 43 years old, and Wang is only 30 years old, which is a joke in society. Li's relatives and friends also ridiculed her for not remarrying. A certain close relative of Li in Ping sent a letter to question her. Li replied in a letter to Ping, the original text said that people's love is ordained by heaven, and its progress is endless. In this civilized world, when new morality is flourishing, widows are allowed to remarry. Remaining a widow and keeping chastity, spending years in hardship, is what foolish women do. You blame me for not remarrying, this is exactly what the wise see wisdom, and the benevolent see benevolence. I am also deeply grateful for your kindness. Although Duke Li treated me kindly, I have served him wholeheartedly for 20 years. Although I dare not say that I have repaid his kindness, I have not failed in the way of a woman. However, Duke Li's bones are not yet cold, and I cannot be tolerated by his descendants. If I do not seek to support myself, how can I survive? You are a discerning person and know the difficulty of my environment, and perhaps you will understand. Even if some people do not understand, I only seek the peace of my heart, what else should I care about? (16th Dispatch)
