Educational News

Under the Cultural Aggression of Violent Japan

Recent Situation of Education in Changchun and Shenyang

Brainwashing Education by the Japanese Can Eliminate Nationalistic Ideas

The Environment Influences People; Northeastern Youths are Gradually Becoming Numb

(Northeast Society) Violent Japan, based on its past experience in Korea, believes that brainwashing education can eliminate nationalistic ideas. Therefore, it is vigorously promoting brainwashing education in the Northeast and understands that the cultural centers of the Northeast are Changchun and Shenyang. Therefore, it is especially exerting efforts in cultural aggression in these areas. How can innocent students deeply understand the cunning and poisonous intentions of the Japanese? In addition, the environment influences people, and they are gradually becoming numb, which is extremely distressing. The situation of brainwashing education in Changchun and Shenyang is recorded separately as follows:

Changchun

(1) In order to unify the educational circles in the Northeast and implement brainwashing education, the Japanese urged the puppet Ministry of Education to establish a teacher training institute (located in the old Jilin No. 2 Normal School in Shuangqiaozi, Changchun). It ordered the puppet education departments of various provinces to select incumbent primary and secondary school teachers and send them to the institute. The subjects of study are the spirit of nation-building, domestic situation, international relations, and Confucian education, among other items. Graduates complete the course in three months. Each person pays a food fee of 50 yuan. During the training period, they continue to receive their original salary. Six classes have graduated so far. The seventh class graduated at the end of last year, and the eighth class has already been selected by the puppet education departments of various provinces according to the instructions of the puppet Ministry of Education. They are required to report on January 7th of this year and start school on the 9th. (2) The puppet Central Army Training Center held a graduation ceremony for the first class of 74 military officers and quartermasters on December 24th of last year. Important puppets from the puppet organization attended in person, and several graduates who had received brainwashing military education gave speeches on their aspirations to strive to implement the puppet government in the future.

Shenyang

(1) The puppet Fengtian Provincial Department of Education received an order from the puppet Ministry of Education to clarify the students from various provinces and cities before the Incident, both government-funded and self-funded, especially paying attention to students studying in Guan Nei (the area south of the Great Wall), fearing that they would resist Japan and oppose Manchukuo. Therefore, it specially formulated an investigation form, which was attached to the puppet order. The deadline was the end of last year to complete the report and submit it to the puppet ministry. The so-called investigation items include: 1. Name of the country of study (those studying in Guan Nei are considered to be "studying in China" and are given special attention with a hostile mentality); 2. Name of the school of study; 3. Subject of study; 4. Number of students studying; 5. Monthly allowance. (2) The puppet Shenyang County Education Bureau, upon receiving a letter from the Japanese Consulate of the "Friendly Nation" (Japan), was ordered by the puppet Ministry of Education to conduct a detailed investigation of the status, occupation, and activities of those from "Manchukuo" who have studied in Japan after returning to the country, as well as a comparison with those who have studied in Europe and the United States, and to submit a report to the relevant cities and counties by the end of February of this year. The investigation items include: 1. Name; 2. School of study; 3. Major subject; 4. Current position, occupation, and activities. (3) The puppet Shenyang County Government, upon receiving an order from the puppet province forwarded by the puppet Ministry of Education, stated that the eighth teacher training session was approaching. The county had a quota of two places and should send trainees to the puppet capital for training. Regarding the selection of trainees in the county, the puppet Education Bureau has selected Wang Chunda, a teacher from the County No. 3 Primary School, and Zhang Junying, a teacher from the Yilukou Primary School. They will soon go to the puppet capital for brainwashing training. In addition, the puppet Shenyang County Government distributes subsidies for brainwashing education to its affiliated primary schools on a quarterly basis, in two installments. Distribution began at the end of last year, with each school receiving 75 yuan in puppet currency. After receiving the funds, the schools have returned to teaching brainwashing education. Furthermore, the puppet Shenyang County Government has stipulated that teachers' salaries be distributed in three grades. In order to encourage teachers to practice teaching brainwashing education, the ninth county affairs meeting of the county decided to newly re-establish the grades into five levels. The salary for the first grade is 32 yuan per month, the second grade is 30 yuan per month, the third grade is 28 yuan per month, the fourth grade is 26 yuan per month, and the fifth grade is 24 yuan per month. The implementation has been announced.

Ministry of Education Dispatches Personnel

To Inspect Qilu University in Jinan

Orders Reorganization of the School's Board of Directors

Rumors of Abolishing the College of Arts and Sciences Denied

(Jinan Correspondence) The private Qilu University in this city has been plagued by unresolved disputes within its board of directors since last year. Students of the College of Arts and Sciences staged two strikes and petitions, which were only resolved this month. Before President Mei Yi-bao arrived, Vice Chairman of the Board Li Zhifan temporarily acted as president. The student roster has now been submitted to the Education Department and forwarded to the Ministry of Education. Due to the repeated disturbances at the university, the Ministry of Education has dispatched Counselor Chen Shicong to Jinan to inspect the school. He also has the task of ordering the reorganization of the school's board of directors.

Reorganizing the Board of Directors (1) Private university boards of directors are organized in accordance with the regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education in October of the 21st year [of the Republic, i.e., 1932]. These regulations placed no restrictions on the number of directors, nor were there strict requirements for their qualifications. The Ministry of Education is now promulgating new regulations that limit the number of directors, with foreign directors not to exceed one-third of the total number. The board must be reorganized in accordance with the new regulations. (2) The division of powers between the board of directors and the president must be clarified. The board of directors should decide on matters to be implemented by the president and should not directly interfere with the president's administration. After arriving in Jinan, Chen has been in contact with the school's board of directors and president. The board of directors will soon be reorganized in accordance with the new regulations. It is reported that the number of directors will be fifteen, with ten Chinese directors and five foreign directors. There will also be strict restrictions on the qualifications of directors.

Inspection of Qilu University Yesterday afternoon at four o'clock, Chen arrived at Qilu University for inspection. He was quite satisfied with the school's management. He also convened a meeting with all faculty, staff, and student representatives to discuss his mission to Jinan. Student representatives asked whether there was any talk of turning Qilu University's College of Arts and Sciences into a rural normal school. Chen said that there was no such thing and urged them to study with peace of mind and not believe rumors. The Ministry of Education is currently most concerned with normal school education, and only national institutions can run normal universities. Private institutions cannot. Qilu University is run by Western friends, and running a normal school would conflict with the Ministry of Education's position. Furthermore, ministry orders require that a university have three colleges to be called a university. If Qilu University were to abolish the College of Arts and Sciences, leaving only the medical school, the university would not be able to exist at all. Moreover, the curriculum of the College of Arts and Sciences is too different from that of a rural normal school. Even if Qilu University has this idea, it must be submitted to the ministry, and the ministry would not approve it. Thus, the students were relieved. The acting president of the school, Li Zhifan, will host a banquet to welcome Chen today (the 15th) at 7:00 PM. Chen will return to Beijing to report on his mission within a few days.

Jiangsu's Social Education Facilities (3)

(Report by Zhou Fo-hai, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Education, at the Provincial Government Memorial Week)

What has been said above are the important social education facilities in Jiangsu in the last two years. We have examined them from many angles and know that most county governments and education bureaus are able to meticulously plan and carry out social education. What deserves our attention most is the attitude of the staff serving in social education organizations. It has fundamentally changed. In the past, everyone thought that serving in social education organizations was very comfortable. Now, this concept has fundamentally disappeared. In the past, everyone did things casually. Now, whenever they do something, they know to draw up a plan in advance and follow it. In the past, attention was only paid to static work, which had nothing to do with the people. Now, they have gradually paid attention to dynamic work, which involves the people. In the past, the work was aimless. Now, everyone knows that standard work is the goal. Although it cannot be said that there are no institutions that are not achieving any results, in general, they have made much more progress than before. However, the staff serving in social education organizations have not yet truly gone to the people. We should also find ways to promote this in the future. Now, let me talk about our current plans.

The first is to redraw the guidance areas of the provincial people's education centers. In the past, the people's education guidance areas under the jurisdiction of the provincial people's education centers had too many counties, making guidance difficult. Now, the six districts have been redrawn into eight districts, and the Provincial Tangshan Farmers' Education Center, originally located in the second district, has been moved to the Nantong district. Another provincial people's education center will be added in the Donghai district to facilitate the guidance work of the provincial people's education centers. This has already been implemented.

The second is to effectively promote the standard work of social education organizations in various counties. Social education organizations in various counties have been able to pay attention to the implementation of standard work. This is a very good sign. However, they are still not very clear about the methods of implementation. Now, we are re-establishing a "Standard Work Promotion Plan" and ordering social education organizations in various counties to follow it. We are also ordering provincial social education organizations to provide effective guidance when guiding social education in various counties.

The second is to implement film education. In order to use film as a tool for implementing social education, we plan to pay special attention to film education this year. In addition to ordering provincial social education organizations to purchase film projectors and travel to various counties to screen films, we also plan to produce several types of films ourselves. The Drinking Water Hygiene, edited by the chairman, has been filmed and completed. Good Friends, Jiangsu Provincial Capital, etc., are being filmed.

The third is to try to combine administration and education. We know that the work done by social education organizations in various counties often overlaps with the work of district offices. As a result, social education organizations cannot fully promote their work due to the lack of political power. District offices cannot achieve satisfactory results due to the lack of educational methods. In order to remedy this shortcoming, we have, in conjunction with the Department of Civil Affairs, designated Kunshan, Yixing, Nantong, and other counties to try to have the director of the farmers' education center concurrently serve as the district chief in order to test the combination of administration and education. If the experiment proves successful in the future, it will be a great way out for our social education.

The fourth is to rectify social education organizations. In the past, the organization of provincial social education organizations was often inconsistent, and the organization of county social education organizations was also inevitably different. Now, we plan to formulate regulations and order a unified organization to facilitate management. Moreover, some county social education organizations have too little funding and cannot develop. We plan to try to increase funding as much as possible so that each institution has at least 2,000 yuan per year. If this cannot be done in the short term, we plan to gradually increase it in the future. As for county institutions with annual funding of more than 3,000 yuan, there is also inevitable waste. We will gradually reduce them in the future. As for other institutions with little achievement, we plan to reduce and merge them as appropriate in order to save money.

Fifth, we actively implement the New Life Movement. The New Life Movement can be said to be the implementation of civic training for the people. Social education organizations should work hard to promote it. We have already formulated a general outline of methods for social education organizations to promote the New Life Movement and ordered social education organizations to earnestly promote it. We will also step up supervision in the future so that the New Life Movement can achieve special results in social education.

In short, there are many areas in Jiangsu social education that need to be improved, and we still need to work hard. (End)

Shanghai Municipal Council

Chinese Middle Schools to Hold Joint Examination

The Shanghai Municipal Council-run Chinese Middle Schools have not yet participated in joint examinations. The Council's Education Committee has organized a subcommittee to consider the method for the Council-run Chinese Middle Schools to hold graduate joint examinations. It is now reported that the committee has submitted three recommendations to the Education Committee: (1) The five Chinese Middle Schools established by the Council should hold a joint examination at a public location in June 1935. The questions should be within the scope of the current curriculum and should have been studied by all the students participating in the examination. There should also be optional or alternative questions so that the scope is sufficient to adapt to the situation of each school. (2) The issue of having external personnel examine certain subjects should be discussed after the above examination has been held, and it is known to what extent the curriculum has been standardized, and how many students from the schools established by the Council are participating in the Shanghai Municipal Middle School Examination. (3) Students should be encouraged to participate in the Shanghai Municipal Middle School Examination. It is reported that the above recommendations have been approved by the Education Committee and adopted by the Board of Directors.

A Short History of the Gangly Boar

— By Qingqu

Sir, surname (Zhu), given name (Luo), born in the year of the Pig, therefore styled (Shi), or it is said that he was born after four months in the womb, and also because he ate unclean food, so he was assigned to (Shi), but it is not known which is true; considering Yang Xiong's Dialects, (Shi, Guandong, also called (　), always lives with the mother hen, which is pleasing to the farmer. The record says (if the (Shi) is fat, then the bristles will be strong and large, (from this, the three words (Gangly Boar) became famous in the world. However, Sir's endowment was foolish and lacking in thought, people thought he was tame and easy to raise, and fed him with bean dregs every day, gradually growing stronger, preventing him from escaping, planting his hat, but Sir slept when he was full, and ate again when he woke up, in less than half a year, he produced children, as many as twenty-four, the keeper was overjoyed, saying, (This is the foundation of wealth,) In the past, Fan Li used animal husbandry to scatter his family wealth three times, calling himself (Duke Zhu), his art was not without reason.

Later, Chen Ping of the Han Dynasty slaughtered his meat and divided it evenly in the community, and eventually became a prime minister. During the Three Kingdoms period, Zhang Yide used this as his career, and was able to become sworn friends with Liu Bei and Guan Yunchang, all of which Sir mediated. It is a pity that Sir is fond of dirt, his residence is called (sty) every day, and the smell is unbearable to approach, but his dung and urine can be used as fertilizer, and crops rely on it. There is nothing to be discarded; although it is like a dirty ruin, it is regarded as a treasure trove.

Sir's body is fat, and his face has many wrinkles. The connoisseur said (almost the appearance of a long life), how can it be the end of the six domestic animals, and they are all inevitable, Muhammad, who saved his life with compassion, and the rest, even if they persuade him to put down the knife, he can become a Buddha on the spot, but in the end he refuses to listen, saying; (If you want to know the world's knives and soldiers, just listen to the sound of the slaughterhouse in the middle of the night,) that is, Sir's last moment; alas! Sir is also pitiful. After Sir died, his corpse was no different from being torn apart, with his shoulders and hooves displayed in the market, and even cut into pieces, those who eat it are naturally unmoved in their hearts. This year's cycle is (Yihai), (Yi), like the shape of a knife, all newborns, according to the zodiac, belong to Sir. Sir is an ominous term, and as an example, the year of Yin belongs to the tiger, which is originally a lion, then those who belong to the pig should be changed to belong to the elephant, which is also possible, but then Sir will rest!

The reporter said, (Zhu Luo), pig slave; in the past, Huang Bi was the president, living in the White House, Wu Zhihui posthumously titled him (fattening pig), which is what pig slave means? However, Zhu Bajie, met Tang Seng, even Sun Wukong, can not do anything; (Gangly Boar), how can there be no Buddha-nature? It is a pity that people do not awaken themselves, but taste the essential meaning of mutual harm in the co-existence of all things.

Rainy Winter Night

— Zhu Ying

The winter night rain is always drifting so unhurriedly, so gently, like fine dust. The electric lights on the telegraph poles are a hazy white, as if shrouded in a thick fog, appearing only as a silent ball of white light as big as a watermelon.

Most of the neon lights in front of the big shops are already extinguished, even though it is only ten o'clock in the evening. Occasionally, one or two shops have not yet turned off their neon lights, but the shop assistants in the counters have their hands in their sleeves, resting on the counters in a daze, quietly listening to the lullabies being broadcast on the radio.

The banners for the winter sale have faded in color from the rain. Water drips from above, green drips, onto the shoulders of hurried and staggering pedestrians.

The streets are so muddy that when cars drive by, sewage flies onto the faces of pedestrians on the sidewalks with the wheels.

The air is so dull; if it weren't for the beggar with a cigarette butt in his mouth and an offensive odor emanating from his body, causing awkwardness behind them, pedestrians might suspect that they were in London, rather than in this first metropolis of the East.

The shouts of the boys selling evening newspapers trembled weakly under the lazily glowing red and green lights at the intersection, trembling on the sparsely populated sidewalks. The evening newspapers were full of moisture and were particularly heavy.

In front of a certain hotel, rickshaw pullers sat on the muddy pedals waiting for customers, idly chatting.

"Damn it, if this rain keeps up for three more days, my whole family will starve to death," one of them muttered.

"Isn't that right? I only pulled eight 'xiaobaokai' yesterday. After paying the rent, I didn't even have money for pancakes. Today, I've only pulled a little over one string of cash..."

Suddenly, a shout of "rickshaw" came from the entrance of the hotel, interrupting their conversation, and they scrambled to push their rickshaws forward.

But apart from one of them who pulled a customer away, the rest remained sitting on the muddy pedals, breathing heavily, watching the unhurried rain drifting like fine dust.

Do Not Repeat Past Mistakes

— Yue

Nine Out, Thirteen Back

— Huang Quan

A few days ago, I saw an article about pawnshops in Europe in the "Chunqiu" magazine, which couldn't help but remind me of the "Nine Out, Thirteen Back" practice in pawnshops in Guangzhou.

What is "Nine Out, Thirteen Back"?

When I was in Guangzhou, I often had to go into pawnshops. My belief was: "Those who pawn and redeem are upper class, those who pawn but don't redeem are middle class, and those who neither pawn nor redeem are lower class." Therefore, I was not ashamed to go into pawnshops, and I dared to discuss prices with the pawnshop clerks and even chat a few extra words.

In my conversations with the clerks, I learned about the so-called "Nine Out, Thirteen Back."

When you take an item to a pawnshop to pawn, it is explained that it can be pawned for one dollar, and the pawn ticket clearly states one dollar, but they only give you ninety cents, giving you a 10% discount for no reason. This is called "Nine Out." When you take the pawn ticket to redeem the item, you need to add thirty cents to them, meaning that to redeem the item early, it will cost you one dollar and thirty cents. This is called "Thirteen Back."

Many times I argued with the pawnshop clerks, but they said, "This is the industry rule, it's up to you whether you want to pawn or not," leaving you with no choice. You only go to pawn things when you are very poor! What choice do you have but to swallow your anger and pawn?

"Nine Out, Thirteen Back" is indeed a practice of heavily exploiting the poor. The Guangdong government has issued orders to prohibit it several times, but most pawnshops still follow it in secret.

Correction: In last Saturday's "Miscellaneous Notes" (Winter in Zizilou), the character "子" (zi) in the title was a mistake and should have been "子" (zi). We hereby correct it.

Royal Fragrance Drifting Record

— Originally by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

This is specifically prepared for beginners in archery! Because in order to require the arrows shot out to have an accurate direction, the first thing that must be emphasized is the posture of shooting; and in order to emphasize the posture of shooting, it is necessary to first pay attention to the position of the two arms, neither too high, nor too low, that is, it is necessary to hold the bow just right. Although the words are very simple, learning it is really very difficult, and it is not something that teachers can teach verbally; you must do your own hard work; if you want to do hard work, these two suspended iron rings are an excellent auxiliary product! Everyone who learns archery cannot hope to improve without relying on them! The reason is that people's shoulders are very easy to move, and when raising the bow, they often cannot avoid being too high, too low, or biased, and cannot always maintain a proper position. So, from the beginning of learning, use these two iron rings to shape him. First, put both hands through the iron rings, so that his shoulders are lifted up by the iron rings. At the same time, the person guiding him should also adjust the length of the two ropes tied to the rings, either raising them a little or lowering them a little, always making them just right, and then handing the bow and arrow to him, letting him learn time after time under the restraint of these two iron rings. The arrow will go through this back door and fall onto the archery lane; at first, it is just random shooting without any target, only seeking to make his posture accurate; after a considerable period of time, his posture will have become natural due to the long-term restraint of the iron rings. In this way, he can leave the iron rings and go to the archery lane to concentrate on learning the method of shooting with targets. You probably never thought that learning archery would require such hard work)!

This is another new lesson we have never heard of before! I really cannot help but secretly admire the Empress Dowager's extensive knowledge! Later, she herself told me that she was able to acquire these scattered and mixed knowledge entirely from reading more books, which shows that reading is a very good habit! (224)

World Rare News

The World's Most Expensive Idol The basement of the Tarragona Municipal Bank in Spain now houses the world's most expensive idol, valued at one million yuan, because this idol was unearthed in the tomb of a child who died three hundred years before the Christian era. It is carved entirely from marble, no more than three inches long, with a face like an ape, exquisite and beloved.

Heavy Taxes on Single People Everyone who has been to Europe knows that single people are not only looked down upon by society, but also subjected to various forms of abuse by the government. Recently, Yugoslavia has enacted a law stipulating that all men and women over the age of thirty who are not married must pay heavy taxes. The Ministry of Communications grants newly married travelers the right to enjoy half-price fares on domestic railways. However, although the country encourages marriage in every possible way, the number of marriages is still not high, which is a symbol of social depression.

Wives and Concubines Sold Cheaply The natives of the Transvaal region of South Africa regard wives and concubines as a major asset. The more they keep, the more solid their assets are said to be. If they are in financial straits, they can transfer them to others, and they can also purchase them at any time when they have money. Recently, due to the global economic downturn, the selling price of wives and concubines has plummeted, and they are not even worth half the price of cattle. Top-quality young women are only sold for a maximum of sixteen pounds, second-quality for ten pounds, middle-aged women between thirty and twenty-five years old for six pounds each, and middle-aged women over thirty years old to thirty-five years old for only two pounds. However, cattle in that area also sell for three pounds each, so people are less valuable than cattle.

World's Highest Telephone There is a small house from Shangmari to Chuabolerezia Mountain in the Alps. There is a telephone installed in this house, which leads to major cities in Europe. The telephone is 9,680 feet above sea level, which is the highest place in the world to install a telephone. Recently, a radio station has been installed outside the house, which will also surpass the height of all radio stations in the world.

World's Largest Family Mr. Jiang Siqi Situnade of the American Box has reached the age of eighty-six, and there are one hundred and twenty-eight people in his family, which is a new record unheard of in the United States. In his sixty-six years of marriage, he has given birth to eleven sons, thirty-six grandsons, seventy-five great-grandsons, and four great-great-grandsons, totaling one hundred and twenty-eight people, including sons-in-law and grandsons-in-law.

City Found in the Desert In the Black Zhilamad area of ​​the southern Arabian Desert, a civilized city was recently discovered by German explorers. This city is in the middle of the desert, looking like a small island. Its construction is very large-scale, the streets are clean, and the drainage facilities are very complete. There are high-rise buildings in the middle, all built of brick and green bricks. The soil around the city is fertile and suitable for various plantings. It is really a natural paradise.

World's Largest Locomotive The St. Gotthard Railway in central Switzerland, which connects with Italy, is now using a locomotive unheard of in the world, because the method of running on steep slopes in mountainous areas uses an 8,800-horsepower electric locomotive. This locomotive weighs 240 tons and can stop suddenly when traveling at a speed of 40 miles per hour. It is equipped with 16 of the latest motors, surpassing the 7,125-horsepower largest locomotive previously boasted by the United States. (Bing Yu)

Prospects for the (Student National Goods Year)

— Xuan Wan

The wheel of time has finally quickly rolled away the disaster-ridden (Women's National Goods Year), and the (Student National Goods Year) that follows has begun to unveil its prelude. From women to students, a new page has been added to the history of the National Goods Movement. Now, let us make a new prospect on the four words (Student National Goods)!

Students are the backbone of society and the reserve force of the knowledge class. Now, we gather the number of students in large, middle, and small schools across the country to promote this national goods movement. This power is of course great, but we must also know that the number of women last year was not small, but the results obtained were like this. Then, for the planned future of this year, we must have a more precise consideration. Obviously, the only bottleneck currently hindering the progress of national goods is that the psychology of worshiping foreign goods has not been abandoned. Women are like this, and students are also like this. Therefore, this point must be recognized first.

According to past facts, university students cannot avoid this (initiation) responsibility for the formation of the psychology of worshiping foreign goods. Whether male or female, they always compete for glory and victory because of their high degree of vanity, beautify the European style, and adopt it as much as possible. From universities to middle schools, from primary schools to society, the whole country is following the trend, leading to the current irreparable situation. Therefore, although we cannot say that the responsibility for the flooding of foreign goods should be entirely borne by the students, at least in the future development of our national products, we must fundamentally cut off this bad psychology.

Therefore, in the prospect of the (Student National Goods Year), the first thing that is needed is a change in the psychology of the students. We must know what time it is now. The dumping of foreign goods has reached the stage of swallowing up the vitality of our entire nation. Do we still want to dream of material enjoyment? To save the nation, we are not even afraid of throwing our heads and spilling our blood. Is it impossible to work together with the people to keep foreign goods a thousand miles away? The students across the country who are standing at the forefront of the times and are rich in knowledge have already had such a deep understanding.

Finally, I have great hope that the students will assume this dual responsibility. The first is to resist foreign goods from the standpoint of consumption, carry out organized publicity, and plan to stop it, (tie the bell and untie the bell), so that the people of the whole country can be transferred to establish confidence in using national goods. The second is to seek the development of national goods from the standpoint of production. Starting this year, we will work harder to explore and research production skills and enrich our knowledge in preparation for serving the society and the country in the future. In this way, our (Student National Goods Year) will not be in vain, and the recovery of the economic crisis will be hopeful.

Plan for Promoting National Goods

— Yang Xie Li

Last year was the Women's National Goods Year, but according to the report released by the customs, the import of luxury goods such as perfumes, cosmetics, and jewelry used by women last year exceeded two million yuan. Therefore, everyone is scolding the Women's National Goods Year for having no achievements! This year is the Student National Goods Year, and this responsibility will be passed on to our students. I think our students are all young and strong, and full of competitiveness. How can we be willing to fall behind and be despised by others! However, everything is valuable to have a plan first, and then there is hope for success. Now, let me talk about my personal plan for promoting national goods.

Before I talk about my plan, I must first explain my background. I am a college student at Wuxi Education College. The Education College is famous in the world for its dedication to public education and its engagement in rural movements. It pays great attention to the development of students' thrifty and hardworking living habits, and stipulates that all students who are about to graduate must go to the countryside for internships and go deep into the people. I am one of those who have been immersed in public education for more than three years and have now come to work in the countryside. Therefore, it is not a problem for us people not to use foreign goods at all. My plan is how to promote national goods among the people? I plan;

(1) To change the people's love psychology The first important thing for us to come to the countryside is to get close to the people, so that the people trust you, and then we can guide them on the right track through subtle influence. We have spent a lot of effort in this area in the months since we came to the countryside, and now we have almost become one with the people, and there is a phenomenon that the people follow us everywhere.

We have always not used foreign goods, as I have already said. In the future, we can further lead by example, purchase and use national goods, change the people's vision, and change the people's psychology, or we can use the people's trust to change customs! Moreover, the so-called (fashion) has no certain standard, but is just a trend of the times. Why is it difficult for us to take using national goods as a fashion?

(2) To improve the people's national concept The people in the countryside have a very weak national concept, so they fundamentally do not know what (national goods) and (foreign goods) are. They are even more inexplicable about the principles of resisting foreign goods and promoting national goods. Therefore, when we educate the people, we must pay attention to improving the people's national concept; we must explain the facts of patriotic people and the historical sites of national heroes to the people. It is best to give the people a general idea of the current international situation and the crisis in our country's future.

(3) To instill in the people the common sense of national goods The people do not pay much attention to the types of foreign goods, and only choose cheap, clever, and beautiful things when buying, so they are most easily exploited by unscrupulous merchants, and often buy foreign goods without knowing it. Therefore, we must help them identify things everywhere, or gather foreign goods for use together with a few families as specimens for the public to visit, reduce the opportunity for the public to be fooled; or collect daily national goods, hold exhibitions, explain their advantages to the people, and instill in them the common sense of national goods.

Safeguarding State-Run Industries

— Zheng

The treatment and protection given by our government to factories operated by foreign merchants is more favorable than those operated by our own people. The donations and taxes borne by foreign-owned factories are often lighter than those of Chinese-owned factories. Therefore, in the market, the products of domestic factories are more expensive. It is difficult to compete with foreign factories. Take sulfuric acid as an example. There are only two factories in Shanghai that manufacture sulfuric acid, one is the Jiangsu Chemical Plant operated by British merchants, and the other is the Kaicheng Acid Plant run by Chinese. The raw materials used by these two factories are imported and taxed in the same way. Kaicheng failed to get an exemption. As for the sulfuric acid produced, the tax levied by the Jiangsu Nitrate and Sulfur Bureau is one yuan per box. The Jiangsu Chemical Plant can refuse to pay because it is operated by foreign merchants. However, the products of Kaicheng must be paid as usual. Therefore, the cost per box is increased by one yuan, and the selling price must be equal to that of foreign goods. Otherwise, it cannot compete for sales. Recently, starting on January 1, the government has increased the spirit tax. All those run by foreign merchants inside and outside the concession do not have to pay, while those run by Chinese merchants must pay as usual. Otherwise, the spirit tax bureau will send staff to the factory to monitor and prohibit sales. As a result, the cost per gallon of Chinese-owned spirit factories is one yuan higher than that of foreign goods. There is no way to compete. The above situation is the opposite of the argument raised by the English-language Greater America Evening News editorial on January 9 that the Chinese government is treating foreign-owned factories harshly. Recently, all countries in the East and West have increased import taxes on products that can be fully supplied by their own country, or the government gives special bonuses to protect them. Therefore, maintaining domestic industry is always considering national defense. All countries in Europe and the United States are adopting this policy to deal with Japan, and Japan is adopting this policy to deal with all countries in Europe and the United States. The biggest reason why domestic industry in China cannot be developed today is that the government has failed to fully implement this protective policy. Unfair words should come from the injured Chinese merchants, not from the privileged foreign merchants. It is strange that tigers and wolves eat cattle and sheep, and the tigers and wolves make a sad sound. What the Chinese people hope from the government is not to drive out tigers and wolves, but to build defensive equipment to protect cattle and sheep from the harm of tigers and wolves. Otherwise, the emerging industry will never have the hope of growing up. How can the country rely on foreign goods to survive? I deeply hope that my authorities will pay attention to it.

Opinions on Using National Goods

— Liu Ping Ji Chen

After years of economic invasion by the great powers, all production enterprises in our country have disintegrated as a result. As far as national goods are concerned, although the government has tried its best to promote them, and people from all walks of life have worked together, such as setting (National Goods Year), (Women's National Goods Year), and (Student National Goods Year) to call on them, the result is still unable to resist the import of foreign goods. The reason for this is mostly that the Chinese people do not like to use national goods. And domestic goods manufacturers and companies also have many shortcomings in terms of production and sales. At the beginning of the Student National Goods Year, all my people, in addition to personally using national goods as an example, should persuade family and friends to advocate national goods together. Here, I will describe my views as far as I can see;

(1) Improve the goods It is well known that domestic goods in our country are durable. However, in terms of manufacturing, they stick to the old methods and do not seek improvement, or they are crudely made and shoddy, and materials are cut corners. Compared with European and American products, they are inevitably inferior. This is why Chinese people abandon domestic goods and buy foreign goods. In the future, domestic goods must be made as exquisite as foreign goods, and even surpass imported goods. National goods sales will increase by leaps and bounds.

(2) Reduce prices National goods are in the budding stage. Due to the dumping of foreign goods and devaluation, those who generally like to use foreign goods are flocking to them. If the prices of national goods are too high, then everyone will stop. We should hold on to the principle of small profits, reduce costs, and make everyone have the impression that national goods are cheap and beautiful. Then, the promotion of national goods will be easier and more effective.

(3) Ensure credibility There are indeed many honest and trustworthy merchants in our country, but occasionally there are one or two merchants who sell inferior goods at high prices, or sell fake goods to counterfeit brands; they do not hesitate to use slippery methods to deal with customers. This kind of behavior completely loses the merchant's moral credibility. The failure of domestic goods is also affected by this. We should set a fixed price, and the goods should be of real value to protect credibility.

(4) Train shop assistants I have seen that in Japanese stores, the staff treat customers with kindness and politeness, doing their best to be polite. On the contrary, the staff in our country's stores treat customers with no sincerity, and even are arrogant, especially the staff in large stores have the worst habits. I think that male and female shop assistants should be strictly trained so that everyone has commercial experience and develops a gentle personality. When customers come, they should be treated warmly and respectfully. If everyone is satisfied, why worry that customers will not be overflowing and guests will feel at home?

(5) The way of publicity Commercial competition is nothing more than publicity. The reason why foreign goods can be sold well in our country's market is mostly due to the two words "publicity." Our country's approach to this is only to brag in advertisements, which has little effect. We should add male and female propagandists who are good at communication and have rich experience to go deep into the people and give practical advice to arouse their patriotism, so that everyone knows it. Oral and paper publicity should be carried out at the same time, then the effect will be significant.

Welcome Student National Goods Year

— Meng Zhao

In a strong country, the people have a natural duty to use their own goods. Only the Chinese need promotion and publicity to use their own goods. It is a shameful thing to say (Let them laugh and scold! I will buy foreign goods myself!). From National Goods Year to Women's National Goods Year, the number of imports of cosmetics and perfumes has become even worse! Promotion and publicity seem to be redundant!

As things change, the (Student National Goods Year) set by various organizations has appeared before our eyes. Who does not know that students are the most sober-minded and patriotic elements who have made contributions? The past May Fourth Movement has left the most glorious page in Chinese history! Therefore, in the (Student National Goods Year), relying on students to be the driving force for selling national goods will surely have very satisfactory results! And students in various commercial organizations should especially unite and stand on the same front!

Interview Notes

Record of an Inspection of the Nanyang Market (2)

— Ji Ping

丨A Conversation with Mr. Kangyuan Xiang丨

(Question) Since the Japanese have expanded the Nanyang market, what countermeasures has the colonial government taken?

(Answer) Apart from the British and Dutch colonies in the Nanyang Islands, such as the American Philippines and French Annam, there have long been extremely high tariff barriers to prevent the large-scale import of goods from non-sovereign states. Therefore, it is difficult for Japan to satisfy its desires in these two places. British Malaya and the Dutch East Indies deeply feel that the dumping of Japanese goods affects the development of their own industries and commerce. Recently, they have successively implemented controlled trade to restrict the import of Japanese goods. Therefore, Japanese goods in the Nanyang market have been greatly impacted, and Japanese merchants have been panicked, and have requested their government to negotiate with the British and Dutch colonial authorities. However, the British government is determined to protect its original market for major industries, such as Lancashire textiles, and therefore seems to have a great determination to restrict the import of Japanese cotton products into British colonies in Nanyang. Therefore, although the Japanese side has protested several times, it has had no effect. As for the Dutch side, since the Dutch East Indies government announced the import restriction law for 56 kinds of commodities, the Japanese side protested severely. In order to ease the sharp conflict, a Japanese-Dutch conference was convened. However, this conference, which has been opened for several months, has been developing and tense at times, but has not made any progress so far. Under this harsh environment, Japan is not willing to sit still and wait for death. It has to find another way in Nanyang to seek a way out for its commodities. They are really thinking hard and striving hard, and as a result, they have obtained a new market with great prospects for expansion. What is this new market? It is Siam. When it comes to Siam, everyone knows that it is the only independent country in Nanyang, located on the Indochina Peninsula northeast of the Malay Peninsula. It has an area of about 195,000 square miles and a population of about 10 million. The people are engaged in agriculture. Except for rice mills and sawmills, other light and heavy industries are extremely backward, so it is the best market for industrial products. Siam also has considerable political contact with Japan in secret. For example, when the League of Nations General Assembly expressed its denial of the puppet state last year, the representatives of all member states unanimously voted against it, while the Siamese representative abstained, expressing goodwill towards Japan. Therefore, when Japan is now restricted by various colonial countries in Nanyang from importing its commodities, it has to expand its market to Siam in order to remedy the situation.

(Question) Now, can the promotion of domestic goods to Nanyang proceed smoothly?

(Answer) I think that if domestic goods want to develop in Nanyang, in addition to striving for excellence and applicability of the goods themselves, the first is to have political power to protect them, the second is to sign commercial treaties with local governments and send envoys and consuls; and the third is to solve the transportation problem. If we Chinese businessmen want to find a way out abroad by relying solely on our own strength, political protection may not be effective. Compared with Japanese businessmen in this regard, we are far behind. There are several places where we have not yet sent consuls to sign commercial treaties (such as Siam and Annam), and there are many obstacles to trade. They can freely levy taxes or reject the import of goods, and you have no way to deal with it. Sometimes, if there are any negotiations, the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce will act expediently, but the Chamber of Commerce is not a diplomatic opponent, how can it speak on behalf of others, and they may not pay attention to it. In my opinion, these two points must be resolved as soon as possible! As for transportation, it is also very important. Japanese goods are transported by Japanese national ships, which can be said to be without any difficulty. Our domestic goods have to rely on foreign ships for transportation, and the freight will of course increase. For example, the freight for Japanese goods to Siam is six yuan per ton, while our domestic goods require 20 yuan, the difference is huge.

(Question) What is the current situation of industry and commerce of overseas Chinese in Nanyang?

(Answer) After the two waves of rubber and tin ore in the Nanyang market in recent years, the market has been very depressed. The large-scale businesses of Chinese businessmen are mostly shaken, especially small businesses, which are not easy to maintain their original state. For example, a tree, the large-scale industry and commerce is the trunk, and the small industry and commerce is the roots. The trunk and the roots are interdependent and help each other. There is no case where the roots are shaken and the trunk does not shake. If you want to strengthen the foundation, you must first cultivate the roots. Therefore, I think these basic forces must be cultivated to be healthy.

New News from the Domestic Goods Industry in a Week

The Nanchang Porcelain Exhibition opened on the 7th, at the Zhongshan Hall of Yuzhang Park. Dozens of companies, including Jiangxi Porcelain Industry Company, Jingdezhen Vocational School, and China Store, participated, and the products were extremely precious.

Tang Zhongming's invention of wood charcoal vehicles has been fully successful. He has invited celebrities from Shanghai to try them out in recent days. The results are very satisfactory, and it is believed that China's current serious gasoline problem can be solved by this in the future.

In order to study industrial production problems and recent trends, the Ministry of Industry specially selected 20 larger factories in Shanghai and sent Qian Desheng to visit them, and asked the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to introduce them separately.

28 Chinese-owned yarn factories have petitioned the government departments and the Shanghai Municipal Government to find ways to maintain the balance of yarn prices and crack down on the monopoly of cotton speculators.

The Nantong Domestic Goods Exhibition opened on the 8th and was extremely enthusiastic. The first day's business was more than 11,000 yuan. The exhibition will last for 20 days and will close on the 27th.

The mobile exhibition organized by the Shanghai Domestic Goods Promotion Association will go to Rugao, Taixing, Qingjiangpu and other places after the Nantong exhibition closes on the 27th.

The Shanghai East China Exhibition has determined the Hujia Muqiao in Hongzhen as the venue, and the arrangements are in place. The opening ceremony will be held on the afternoon of the 15th. A total of more than 60 manufacturers participated.

The temporary commercial market of the Shanghai North China Exhibition was fully opened on the 15th.

The International Trade Bureau introduces domestic pig bristles to New York, USA. The products from Sichuan are the best and are most welcome in the European and American markets. Exporters can contact the bureau immediately.

The Shanghai Sugar Industry Association has set up a sugar industry cooperative joint-stock company to promote domestic sugar. The address is 129 Minguo Road, and the opening ceremony is scheduled for February.

Free Talk

Spring Grass and Poetry

— Ruo Wu

Mr. Jing'an Wang wrote this in "Human Words on Poetry": (People know that Hejing's "Dian Jiang Chun", Shunyu's "Su Mu Zhe", and Yongshu's "Shao Nian You" are three masterpieces for chanting spring grass, but they do not know that the five words "fine rain wets flowing light" by Zhengzhong came first, which can capture the soul of spring grass.) This is of course a very worthwhile remark. Spring grass in poetry is really full of imagery. In the time of February and March in Jiangnan, looking at the lush grass, it is easy to make people feel a kind of desolate loneliness. Writing about spring grass can be said to be a characteristic of Chinese literati, perhaps due to temperament and environment! In addition to the few verses Wang mentioned, we can also see Qin Shaoyou's ("Leaning on a dangerous pavilion, hatred is like fragrant grass, lush and endless.") and Mei Shengyu's another verse chanting grass "Shao Nian You"; ("The railing twelve alone by spring, the clear blue extends to the clouds, thousands of miles, February and March, the journey is bitter and sad.") are all full of a faint sense of sorrow. As for Li Meixi's "Liu Yao Ling" in the Yuan Dynasty ("Vaguely distant fragrant grass, dyed the spring breeze green.") is good, but the artistic conception is completely different. In the nineteen ancient poems, ("Green grass by the riverbank") and ("Looking around, what is vast, the east wind shakes the grass.") are both sentences that evoke a sense of life. There are no abstract explanatory words such as resentment and hatred in it, but the poet's inner feelings are conveyed through concrete images, so that readers get an irresistible impression of desolation. The famous sentences of the Wei and Jin Dynasties ("Spring grass grows in the pond.") and ("Spring grass is blue.") are also written very naturally. Later, Wang Zhou's ("Spring grass is green at will, without anyone.") and Bai Juyi's ("The green grass skirt waist is a diagonal.") can also convey the subtle lyric interest in short sentences. Later, in the lyrics of the Southern Song Dynasty, we often see lyrics dedicated to chanting spring grass, and most of them are long tunes. In terms of arrangement and antithesis, there is certainly no lack of excellent skills, but they are all inevitably in the style of "Xishe" carving. Therefore, whenever we read very long rambling lyrics, we feel that the chanting of objects is indeed very "skillful", but the overall impression left to the reader is not as good as some short sentences in the past. From this, we can see that arrangement and allusion are enough to damage the unity and completeness of art. Recently, I read Lu Jiye's "Ji Ruo Sui", the first "Banqiao Xing" is a six-character poem, and the sentences are; ("Spring goes and the grandson's dream is old, spring comes and the emperor's soul disappears, seventy-two families of fragrant grass, I don't know where the long bridge is.") It can also express a kind of dreamlike loneliness in spring.

In fact, there are really too many poems and lyrics chanting spring grass. As for Liu Chang's of the Song Dynasty ("Spring grass is continuous and cannot be named, hidden in the water and the origin of the stream, it seems to dislike the prosperous place of cars and horses, and it will not be born as soon as it enters the city gate.") and Wang Anshi's ("Fragrant grass knows who planted it, and there are several clumps along the steps. There is no intention to compete with the times, why is it green and lush?") are all works that are intended to express something other than spring grass. This is not writing about spring grass but writing about people. I personally like sentences that do not specifically chant spring grass but depict the spirit of spring grass. In March of late spring, the grass grows in Jiangnan, there are swallows, distant trees, sunsets with afterglow, and pedestrians drifting like dreams. Looking at that piece of blue, it really brings a kind of indescribable loneliness and joy. As long as a few lines of poetry slip from the mouth, it has drawn us into the pastoral spring dream of ancient poets.

However, this is too far from the present century. Our new poets should look at spring grass with new eyes and new emotions, and express it with new techniques.

Literati Seem to Sign a Contract with Poverty

— Jiang Ji Ping

Literati seem to sign a contract with poverty. If we open the books of ancient and modern China and foreign countries, we can find that nine out of ten literati are poor. The day before yesterday, I read Ishikawa Takuboku's "Two Bloodstains" (translated by Zhou Zuoren), and I was quite touched by the author's introduction at the back. Takuboku was a primary school teacher in Shibumin Village, Japan, with a monthly salary of eight yuan, and often felt the difficulty of life. The writings of literati are very related to his environment. In "Two Bloodstains", there is a very pitiful, very thin, and very poor child, Shintaro, who may be Takuboku's own microcosm, because he himself suffered from lung disease. His poverty was such that he could not plan for medical expenses, and he often ran out of food. Later, he published a collection of songs ("Sad Toys"), which sold for only 20 yuan, and he bought the tonic he wanted to eat on weekdays. I am afraid that the medicine could not cure his inner melancholy. Before he had finished eating the tonic, he passed away. He was only twenty-seven years old when he died. American novelist Hawthorne published his first book, but no one read it, and as a result, he was impoverished. He no longer wanted to make a living by writing, so he ran to the Salem Customs to work. Later, he lost his job again, and comforted by his wife, he stayed at home and wrote "The Scarlet Letter", and became famous in one fell swoop. Cervantes was also very poor, wearing ragged clothes and owing a lot of debt. Zhou Zuoren himself has an essay on Cervantes in "The Garden"; ("On November 8, 1590, Cervantes, in order to get forty yuan worth of cloth on credit, signed a contract with the cloth shop with his guarantor, and there were four notaries as mediators, which was as solemn as guaranteeing public bonds, as the legend says. When the government asked him to return the embezzled public funds in the winter of 1601, he also (had no means to feed himself), so he was imprisoned the following year. He was so poor, which is really possible. There is also a writer, I forgot his name, who was so poor that he sold everything, and later simply had no home to return to, so he wandered on the road at night. On the one hand, we feel sorry for this poor writer, but on the other hand, this matter is very interesting.

Most of the Chinese poets are also poor, such as Li Bai's ("Five-flower horse, thousand-gold fur, call the boy to bring out fine wine, and spend myriads of sorrows with you.") is really rare. Therefore, it makes me think that poetry and prose become more ingenious when they are sad, perhaps there is some reason for it. Because of the stimulation of poverty, there must be a kind of abnormality in the nerves, so the poems and prose written are mostly profound. Or he wanted to borrow the comfort of the article, and his thoughts entered a mysterious and ethereal realm, and became a romantic school. Therefore, the poverty of literati is also a major factor in the success of his article.

Poverty is considered a very noble thing by Chinese literati. Tu Chishui of the Ming Dynasty was also very poor. His wife told him that there was no rice to cook tomorrow, but he said; ("Tomorrow's affairs, there will be tomorrow, and do not fail the moonlight of the parasol tree.") This is really helpless optimism, but the psychology of taking poverty as nobility can also be seen faintly.

My Cousin

— Ouyang Shan

If you want to predict the future destiny of a nation's children, primary school teachers should be a worthy object of study.

Ten years ago, when I ran to the provincial capital for the first time from the countryside, I was still a child who felt strange about everything. My cousin hated me very much, saying ("Since you were born in the countryside, you should die in the countryside.") Later, seeing that I was not dull to a very terrible degree, he became kind to me and taught me everything.

("In the world, if you ignore a nail, you can't be said to be paying attention to it properly. Help me with some heavy housework. Whenever you have time, take out this box of books and read each one twice! A Xing (the name of his son) is useless. He would rather use his hands than his brains.")

At that time, he was working as an assistant teacher in a small school. Because sometimes he had to be in arrears with his salary, or issue discounted banknotes, he never received the full amount of 22 yuan. Every time he came back from receiving money, he stamped his feet and angrily scolded the education industry and all the people who were active in it, vowing to change his career, saying that even going to be a useless clerk or recorder.

He was very timid and had no friends, and even the hobby of drinking tea that any Cantonese had never contracted. He got up early, according to the norms set by hygienists for all healthy and wealthy people to abide by; he also followed the instructions of that norm and went to bed at a certain appropriate time. In winter, he ate an extra bowl of cured meat rice prepared by his cousin in the morning. Except for the days when he was paid, he didn't even smoke raw cigarettes, and he didn't talk much. He lived like a mouse, cautious, quiet, and regular.

Even he himself admitted that the only shortcoming, which he did not make up his mind to correct, was that he liked to play small mahjong. Coincidentally, a few pale-faced humble colleagues came, and they gambled together and told all kinds of old jokes. Unlike enthusiastic young people, he was not an addicted and generous gambler. But when he played cards, he was very serious; bending over, paying attention to every small colorful card with his sick eyes, his forehead and nose were covered with sweat; sometimes he argued for half an hour to criticize a card's mistake.

When his father was seriously ill, because he talked to the son of his deceased brother about the separation of the family, he quarreled and beat each other fiercely. Afterwards, he shivered all over, his eyes flashing with melancholy light, and he murmured to himself; What a fool! Have I ever done anything to be sorry for anyone? What crime have I committed? What happened to this world? Even if I meet Yama, I can't find any other flaws except saying that I like to play cards······"

He lived in a prison room cast in purple copper. Accompanied by small indignation and curses, he used all words to explain his actions, but refused to release himself; cut off various risky thoughts, and rejected the thoughts and theories that could make human progress. Seeing the drastic changes in society, he smiled, as if watching the gradual decline of his neighbor's family fortune, and said his ridiculous conclusion;

(As long as people's hearts are not dead, everything will return to its original state.)

What is lacking here is; I don't know how he taught those pure and innocent children when he was in class.

The Human World (2)

— Li Huiying

At this time, I was watching the figure of my old friend in the dark, while waiting for his reply, waiting for him to answer how much more I had to walk, or where he would lead me. But he did not answer me, but went deeper into a dark alley. There was not a single light on the road, as if it was isolated from the city. The alley was about three feet wide. As for how the ground was, whether it was wet or dry, my myopic eyes could not distinguish it at all. Therefore, due to the unsteady steps, I added different sounds to the dark alley. However, it was strange, my old friend walked so skillfully, which made me determine that he was not intentionally deceiving me. But since he did not answer me for a long time, I could not help but ask again;

(Friend, why can't we get there no matter how much we walk, what's going on? Moreover, we always walk on dark roads, where are you going to lead me?)

(Okay, don't be verbose. We're here).

After he finished speaking, he stopped and knocked eight times in a row on a small door nailed with slats in a regular manner. I also stopped and waited.

(This is a secret agency)!

As soon as I thought about it, I immediately thought of the terrible dark cave in detective novels. However, no matter what, I was sure that my friend would not harm me, which made me feel relieved and emboldened. Waiting, waiting for a while to appreciate the scenery inside.

This alley is simply like hell. Although I have never been to hell, from the general discussion, it seems that no one denies that hell is dark. But, where can this go? Let me think about it; we started from 15th Street, walked on Zhengyang Street, and turned into 2nd Street, then this should be a small alley near 2nd Street. It's too secluded. Standing in the dark alley, you really can't think that outside is the prosperous Harbin City.

After waiting for a while, there was no movement. My friend knocked eight times again. Yes, it was absolutely true that he knocked eight times again, no more, no less.

A slight sound of footsteps came from a distance and stopped in front of the slat door. A little girl of thirteen or fourteen years old opened the door. After we stepped over the threshold, the slat door was closed immediately. The courtyard was also a piece of black like the alley. The house was also black. After turning a corner, I followed my friend into a dark room.

Random Notes on the Journey to Guizhou (Part 1)

— You Qi

Passing Lou Mountain Pass

In the morning when the sun has not come out, in this mountain valley, it is always gloomy, shrouded in smoke and fog all over the sky.

The mountains cannot be seen to the end, layer upon layer, with thick clouds rising from the mountainside, like cotton, floating in the sea and sky. If the inn where you live is close to the top of the mountain covered with clouds, then you can smell a peculiar smell, which is said to be miasma.

Roosters seem to be particularly numerous in this village and town. One crows, and all around echo. There is no need to look at what time it is. The sky is about five o'clock. This, you have to hurry up and get up, and prepare to set off. The first step of getting up is to stand at the door of the inn and watch the sky all around, because in the hearts of travelers, they firmly remember this sentence;

丨丨It is not too late to stay overnight before dark, and look at the sky early when the rooster crows.

If the weather is not good, the muddy mountain roads washed by rain will have a great impact on travelers. But today, it's okay. Although the sky is heavy, that's normal. In the gloom, there seems to be no sign of rain. Well, today is considered lucky again.

It is exactly the end of summer. The sultry heat in the mountain valley during the day is a bit scary. When staying overnight, the coolies who are attacked by fatigue are naturally too lazy to sleep in the prison-like inn. Here, under the porch of the inn, it becomes a drawing of meat, lying full of people in a mess. The ochre-brown body is lined with the grayish-yellow soil, and the color is very moving.

(Get up, hurry up, the rooster has crowed three times!) The head coolie shouted, opening his broken and hoarse throat. This seems to have become a routine business, and the head coolie is familiar with this routine.

The coolies got up in a panic, rubbing their eyes that had not slept enough, and a wave of resentment welled up on their faces.

(Boss lady, here, this is two hundred coins, even for today's breakfast.) (Saying) while speaking, a large rough-patterned quilt was thrown in, and several copper coins worth fifty wen were placed on the counter.

The boss lady is smiling, and several crow's feet that have been weathered for a long time are moving at the corners of her eyes.

Really, this seems to have become a task. No matter which inn you stay in, there is always such a riot every morning.

Wash your face by the stone pool for feeding donkeys, some also wash their feet by the way, then casually gnaw two bowls of coarse rice, and start to move. The sedan chair, the sliding pole, (Note) the flower basket pole, are carried from the frame built by the roof beams to the front of the inn door. That is just an empty frame. The oilcloth (Note) of the shop and the cushion for sitting must be temporarily laid. However, although the things have been carried to the front of the door, people have quietly dispersed. What is the reason? To prepare strength.

(Preparing strength) is not doing morning exercises, nor is it practicing any boxing, but to lie on a bamboo bed inlaid with wooden planks, and use the long gun of the bamboo tube and a half-dark oil lamp to invigorate the strength.

This is not surprising. Cigarettes are sold so expensive. The goods that are despised in the metropolis, such as Big Knife brand and Red Peach brand, have to be sold for more than two hundred a box here. It goes without saying that the good ones may not be available. Datou, on the other hand, is a local specialty. A small pot made of purple-red pottery, filled with a pot, weighs three qian, and the color is very good, and the selling price is two hundred coins, which is fair enough.

Good Location

— TK

The March Gold Bar Tender Market Presents an Uncertain State

Initially Rising Due to Extraordinary Foreign Exchange Tightness

Subsequently Returning Due to Buyers Emerging

Yesterday, the March gold bar market initially rose due to the plummet in exchange rates. Suddenly, Mobil Oil had a settlement, leading to extraordinary tightness in US exchange rates, stirring up a buying frenzy, and causing the long positions to aggressively increase their stakes, leading to a rapid rise. Unexpectedly, after the foreign exchange market tightened, it suddenly eased, and general buyers emerged after entering. Although the Central Bank frequently opened spot tenders, the market supply exceeded demand, finally breaking the 70-yuan mark, performing even worse than before the swap. In the early morning, overseas silver markets saw British silver rise and US silver remain flat, while forward silver prices fell, and foreign exchange rates plummeted considerably. London raw gold rose five pence. Off-market forward trading was slightly stable, rising to 71.2 yuan, because the swap was offered by the long positions at a premium of more than seven yuan. It then rose to over two yuan. The Central Bank announced its posted rates, with both British and US rates rising by 0.125, while the Customs Gold Unit fell by 0.008, and the standard gold bar price retreated to 994.5 yuan, slightly declining. After opening, general sentiment, in light of the decline in British and US exchange rates but the rise in British-French rates, saw this as a phenomenon of the US dollar being uniquely expensive and expected extraordinary tightness in the foreign exchange market. As expected, banks opened by grabbing US dollars, boosting confidence, and large clients had strong buying appetites. The long positions scrambled to increase their stakes, immediately causing prices to rise. Although there was fluctuation, the sudden settlement by Mobil Oil led to an even tighter foreign exchange market and a relatively brisk rise. Floating short positions were rapidly closed at high prices, but a surge in selling at high prices stirred up the supply, gradually causing a pullback. The announcement of the silver equalization tax remained unchanged, still levied at 6%, calculated at one shilling five pence 7.1875, also lacking impact. Afterwards, the selling side became more enthusiastic and relatively weak. Although there was a decline, the Central Bank opened spot tenders at 965 yuan, and after the low price, large clients bought aggressively, making it easy to rebound. However, as exchange rates gradually hardened, the supply side continued to work hard, and those increasing their stakes, seeing the unfavorable situation, exited together. Despite some trying to maintain at the lower level, prices ultimately retreated within the 70-yuan mark. The afternoon close was the weakest, with the overall trend uncertain for half a day, turning from firm to weak. The buying side's psychology was difficult to sustain, leading to this outcome. The near-term selling price opened in the morning, with the British pound at 1 shilling 5 pence 0.1875 and the US dollar at 34.75 yuan, compared to the previous close, showing the British pound weakening by 0.0625 and the US dollar tightening by 0.125. The US Dollar Rises Sharply, and the New York Stock Market Falls Across the Board

A report from Xinfeng Foreign Firm stated that yesterday (the 15th), the New York stock market fell sharply due to widespread anxiety and fear caused by the imminent Supreme Court ruling on the gold coin clause case. It only slightly rebounded higher in the last half hour. Trading was especially smooth, and the telegraph was three minutes behind the market. Gold and silver mining stocks fell the most severely, and wheat and other commodities all created new lows for the quarter. The most significant event of the day was the sharp rise of the US dollar against foreign exchange. News from Europe stated that if the Supreme Court's ruling to uphold the gold coin clause were seriously considered, the United States would restore the former US dollar and therefore purchase US dollars. The currencies of the countries in the New York Gold Group fell by 17 to 101, and most have fallen below the shipping point, so the United States can now import gold. In Paris, the US dollar created the highest record since 1933. In London, the British pound fell sharply below the former parity, and the Dutch currency also fell sharply. The rebound at the end of the stock market was a natural reaction after the sharp fall. The bond market was weak, except for US government bonds, and Dutch bonds fell particularly sharply. Royal Dutch Shell's 4% bonds due in 1945 fell by 16 yuan the day before due to the ruling by the Hague Court, and continued to fall by 13.5 yuan yesterday. Before the opening of the bidding, Indian cotton continued to rise, while American cotton fell. Selling pressure was slightly strong, and the three major long positions of Tongxing, Changfeng, and Changhe closed out a significant amount of their positions. Therefore, the market situation appeared quite weak, and sentiment was dampened. However, the spot month market was tight due to delivery issues, while the distant month market fell by five points. In the afternoon opening, it was heard that gold prices closed lower and were weak. However, those who profited covered their positions in the third session, and because those who had open positions covered their shorts this month, the market turned firm. Prices for all months rose by five points to one dime. It is noted that the following were sold: Tongxing 4,000 bales, Gengfeng 900 bales, Changfeng 3,500 bales, Runkang 1,200 bales, Yikang 1,000 bales, Yuanxingchang 3,200 bales, Changhe 3,200 bales. The following were bought: Yuanda 1,100 bales, Dafu 1,500 bales, Zhenda 1,700 bales, Gengfeng 1,000 bales, Yuande 2,100 bales, Yongchang 800 bales. Uncertain Gold Bar Proposal, Large-Scale Closing of American Cotton Long Positions

Yesterday, American cotton opened higher due to favorable overseas market conditions and strong demand from peers. Afterwards, due to the uncertainty surrounding the gold bar proposal, a large number of long positions were closed, and the market gradually declined. At the same time, the gold yuan sharply rose, and grains and the stock market were weak, which also contributed to the unfavorable market situation. However, peers showed strong buying interest when prices fell. Near the close, the market was slightly better due to silver coins. The spot market was quiet. Spot prices fell by 10 points, and futures fell by 9 to 15 points. The British cotton market was stable, with spot prices up 6 points and futures up 2 points. Indian cotton speculators bought, Japanese merchants sold, and there was some arbitrage. Pingguo'er rose by 2.5 cents, Aomula rose by 1 rupee, and Bairofexi rose by 2.75 rupees. Source: Telegram from London, 15th.

Japanese Yarn Aggressively Invades China: Price Comparison Table

In recent years, high cotton prices and low yarn prices have caused significant distress to mills. It is often heard that some businesses are unable to sustain operations. It is rumored in the market that some mills are considering early shutdowns and delayed restarts during the lunar new year period, indicating the seriousness of the situation for Chinese mills. The yarn market should have an active upward trend, but unfortunately, due to financial constraints and the low prices of Japanese yarn, the North China market has already been seized by Japanese yarn. It is noted that the market price for 42-count Japanese Shuiyue yarn is 32 yuan lower than Chinese Jincheng yarn. Although the goods have slight differences, the price difference is alarming. The prices of other 32-count, 16-count, and 20-count yarns are all more than ten yuan or five, six, seven, or eight yuan lower than Chinese yarns.
